The Scavenger’s Wake (Asynchronous Rogue-lite)  
The Hook: You are a drone operator exploring a massive, persistent graveyard of derelict ships left behind by a galactic war.  
	•	Gameplay: Unlike traditional RPGs, you don’t control a person; you control a remote drone with a limited battery. You click through rooms of a ship (procedurally generated) to find scrap.  
	•	Browser Strength: Perfect for "tab-gaming." You can set your drone to "Auto-Scan" a sector while you work in another tab.  
	•	The Twist: The "Wake" is persistent. If a player dies in a specific sector, their ship becomes a "ghost wreck" that other players can scavenge for high-tier loot.

Questions  
Single player?

Ability to mine asteroids  
Need to protect cargo from other miners or pirates  
Skill levels  
Ability to visit other locations \- public viewing platform ?  
Character improvement thru skill tree  
Salvage of items contributes to tech tree  
Buy sell upgrade miner drones  
Print delivery engines?  
Build tree based on mined elements \- bamboo

Cb \- celestial body

State of known cbs managed by server.    
Scan of unknown environment creates new cbs  
Clients request server to scan \- payload of cbs returned

Starting  
At a planet? At a moon? At the asteroid belt?

Repair?

Crafting hierarchy 

This hierarchy follows a logical progression from raw atomic materials to complex sub-assemblies, eventually reaching the pinnacle of self-sustaining, automated stellar-mining technology.

having both expendable and permanent units adds a great layer of tactical depth. You'll have to balance "suicide runs" for rare, volatile materials against the steady, reliable output of your veteran fleet.

Here is the finalized 50-level hierarchy for a **Drone-Logic Economy**, categorized by their functional role in the fleet.

---

## **Tier 1: Scavenger Swarms (Levels 1–10)**

*Focus: High-turnover, expendable units for surface mining.*

| Level | Item | Cost (Material \+ Unit Type) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| 1 | **Raw Regolith** | 1x Basic Scrap \+   |
| 2 | **Iron & Nickel Ingots** | 5x Regolith \+ 10u Thermal Energy |
| 3 | **Basic Silicates** | 3x Regolith \+ Fine Mesh Filter |
| 4 | **Copper Wiring** | 2x Copper Ore \+ 1x Extruder Tool |
| 5 | **Steel Plating** | 3x Iron Ingot \+ 1x Forge Logic Chip |
| 6 | **Solid Fuel Pellets** | 2x Carbon \+ 1x Chemical Mixer |
| 7 | **Hydrazine Propellant** | 3x Ammonia \+ 1x Fuel Synth Module |
| 8 | **Reinforced Glass** | 4x Silicates \+ 1x Pressure Chamber |
| 9 | **Basic Hydraulics** | 2x Steel Plating \+ **Permanent "Loader" Arm** |
| 10 | **Industrial Drill Bit** | 5x Steel \+ **Expendable "Borer" Unit** |

---

## **Tier 2: Logistics & Maintenance (Levels 11–20)**

*Focus: Permanent support units that repair the expendable swarms.*

| Level | Item | Cost (Material \+ Unit Type) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |

| 12 | **Silicon Wafers** | 5x Silicates \+ Argon Gas |
| 13 | **Circuit Boards** | 1x Silicon Wafer \+ 2x Copper Wiring |
| 14 | **Oxygen Scrubbers** | 2x Lithium \+ 1x Filter Frame |
| 15 | **Solar Cell Sheets** | 2x Silicon \+ 1x Silver Contact |
| 16 | **Thermal Radiators** | 5x Copper \+ 1x Heat Sink |
| 17 | **Battery Cells** | 3x Lithium \+ **Permanent "Battery" Drone** |
| 18 | **Tungsten Carbide** | 2x Tungsten \+ 3x Carbon |
| 19 | **Electromagnetic Coils** | 10x Copper \+ 1x Iron Core |
| 20 | **Automated Sifter** | 5x Steel \+ **Permanent "Sorter" Unit** |

---

*Focus: Self-replicating swarms and planetary-scale equipment.*

| Level | Item | Cost (Material \+ Unit Type) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| 41 | **Antimatter Containment** | 10x Grapples \+ **Permanent "Trap" Drone** |
| 42 | **Nano-Swarm Hives** | 100x Assemblers \+ **Expendable "Devourer" Swarm** |
| 43 | **Dark Matter Refiner** | 1x Antimatter \+ 1x Void Siphon |

| 47 | **Hard-Light Projectors** | 10x Pulse Lasers \+ **Expendable "Shield" Wall** |
| 48 | **Transmutation Chamber** | 1x Dark Matter Refiner \+ 1x Lead Batch |
| 49 | **Chronos-Stabilizers** | 1x Singularity Core \+ **Permanent "Stasis" Drone** |
| 50 | **The Star-Eater Drill** | 10x Nano-Hives \+ **The Hive-Mind (Final Hub)** |

---

### **Fleet Strategy Tips**

* **The "Dart" Loop:** Use cheap level 1-10 expendable drones to gather the raw resources needed to build the permanent Level 11+ support fleet.  
* **Repair Overhead:** Permanent drones require "Maintenance Kits" (crafted at Level 13\) to stay functional, or they eventually degrade into Level 1 Scrap.  
* **Late-Game Efficiency:** Once you hit Level 42 (**Nano-Swarm Hives**), you can set your "Devourer" swarms to auto-recycle expendable drones into raw materials, creating a closed-loop economy.

---

## **Tier 1: The Foundation (Levels 1–10)**

*Focus: Basic mineral extraction and simple alloy smelting.*

1. **Raw Regolith:** Crushed asteroid rock.  
2. **Iron & Nickel Ingots:** Purified metallic chunks.  
3. **Basic Silicates:** Processed glass and insulation.  
4. **Copper Wiring:** The backbone of early power systems.  
5. **Steel Plating:** Basic structural reinforcement.  
6. **Solid Fuel Pellets:** Early chemical propellant.  
7. **Hydrazine Propellant:** Refined liquid rocket fuel.  
8. **Reinforced Glass:** Pressurized viewing ports.  
9. **Basic Hydraulics:** Mechanical movement for mining arms.  
10. **Industrial Drill Bit:** The first Tier 0 mining tool.

---

## **Tier 2: Orbital Infrastructure (Levels 11–20)**

*Focus: Electronics, life support, and energy management.*

11. **Lead Shielding:** Protection against cosmic radiation.  
12. **Silicon Wafers:** The start of advanced computing.  
13. **Circuit Boards:** Basic logic gates and controls.  
14. **Oxygen Scrubbers:** Simple atmospheric recycling.  
15. **Solar Cell Sheets:** Low-yield energy generation.  
16. **Thermal Radiators:** Managing heat in a vacuum.  
17. **Battery Cells:** Early energy storage.  
18. **Tungsten Carbide:** Heat-resistant drilling components.  
19. **Electromagnetic Coils:** For moving heavy loads.  
20. **Automated Sifter:** First-generation automated ore separation.

---

## **Tier 3: Deep Space Exploration (Levels 21–30)**

*Focus: Rare earths, lasers, and precision engineering.*

21. **Titanium Alloy:** Lightweight, high-strength hull plating.  
22. **Gold-Plated Contactors:** High-efficiency electronics.  
23. **Excimer Lasers:** Precise cutting tools for hard rock.  
24. **Micro-Processors:** Complex drone AI control.  
25. **Cryogenic Tanks:** Handling super-cooled gases.  
26. **Plasma Torches:** Cutting through exotic ores.  
27. **Superconductors:** Zero-resistance power flow.  
28. **Carbon Nanotubes:** Molecularly reinforced cables.  
29. **Magnetic Grapples:** For tethering to low-gravity asteroids.  
30. **Pulse Mining Laser:** High-efficiency thermal extraction tool.

---

## **Tier 4: The Tech Revolution (Levels 31–40)**

*Focus: Fusion, gravity manipulation, and exotic matter.*

31. **Deuterium Fuel:** Fuel for fusion reactors.  
32. **Fusion Core:** High-output energy generation.  
33. **Ion Thrusters:** Long-range asteroid hauling engines.  
34. **Graphene Sheets:** Ultra-thin, ultra-strong shielding.  
35. **Neural Link Interface:** Enhanced manual mining precision.  
36. **Gravimetric Sensors:** Detecting ore veins deep underground.  
37. **Inertial Dampeners:** Moving massive rocks without shaking the ship.  
38. **Quantum Relays:** Instantaneous data transfer for remote mining.  
39. **Molecular Assemblers:** Self-repairing mining equipment.  
40. **Sonic Resonator:** Shattering asteroids using high-frequency vibration.

---

## **Tier 5: Future-Tech Mastery (Levels 41–50)**

*Focus: Singularities, nanites, and stellar-scale engineering.*

41. **Antimatter Containment:** Storing the universe's densest energy.  
42. **Nano-Swarm Hives:** Millions of bots that "eat" asteroids.  
43. **Dark Matter Refiner:** Processing exotic energy sources.  
44. **Spatial Fold Drive:** Instant travel to distant asteroid belts.  
45. **Monopole Magnets:** Perfect ore attraction and sorting.  
46. **Singularity Core:** Infinite power for massive industrial rigs.  
47. **Hard-Light Projectors:** Creating temporary tools out of pure energy.  
48. **Transmutation Chamber:** Turning common lead into rare iridium.  
49. **Chronos-Stabilizers:** Speeding up the mining process through time dilation.  
50. **The Star-Eater Drill:** A planetary-scale harvester capable of deconstructing entire moons and siphoning solar plasma.

To craft the **Extruder Tool** (Level 4), the player needs to transition from simply smashing rocks to shaping materials. Since this is an early-tier item, the process is straightforward but requires a specific "Recipe" and a "Fabrication Station."

In a drone-based economy, crafting isn't just about clicking a button; it’s about assigning the right resources to a production line.

---

## **The Extruder Tool Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

To assemble one Extruder Tool, your drones must collect and process the following:

* **2x Copper Ore:** Mined by your **Level 1 "Dart" Drones** from asteroid veins.  
* **1x Iron Ingot:** Processed at a **Solar Smelter** (Level 2\) using raw Iron ore.  
* **10 units of Energy:** Generated by your base or a **Battery Drone** (Level 17\) if you're crafting in deep space.

### **2\. The Crafting Process**

The player must follow these steps in the UI or at their Orbital Workshop:

1. **Smelt:** Feed the raw Iron into the furnace to create the tool's casing.  
2. **Draw:** Feed the Copper Ore into a **Level 4 Extruder Module** (if you have a permanent one) or a manual "Starter Kit" bench.  
3. **Assembly:** The Iron Ingot is shaped into a die-cast, and the Copper is pulled through it to create the **Copper Wiring** required for the next level.

---

## **Role in the Hierarchy**

The **Extruder Tool** is a "Logic Gate" for your progression. Without it, you cannot create Level 4 **Copper Wiring**, which is a primary ingredient for:

* **Level 13 Circuit Boards** (The brain of every drone).  
* **Level 16 Thermal Radiators** (Prevents your drones from overheating).  
* **Level 19 Electromagnetic Coils** (Used for heavy lifting and propulsion).

---

## **Black Box Recovery (Your Mechanic)**

Since you mentioned using **expendable** drones, if the drone carrying your Extruder Tool is destroyed:

* **Recovery:** You can send a Scavenger drone to the wreck site.  
* **Yield:** You will recover a **"Damaged Extruder"** (worth 50% of the Iron and Copper) or, if you're lucky, the **Black Box**, which instantly restores the **Blueprint** data so you don't have to re-research it.

Would you like to define a specific "Failure Rate" for crafting these early tools, or should it always be 100% successful if you have the materials?

The **Fine Mesh Filter** (Level 3\) is a critical early-game component. While "Dart" drones can smash asteroids into Raw Regolith, the filter is what allows your automated systems to sift through that dirt to find the high-value **Basic Silicates** needed for glass and electronics.

In your drone-based economy, the blueprint focuses on structural integrity and microscopic precision.

---

## **Fine Mesh Filter Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **3x Iron Ingots:** Used to create the structural frame and the ultra-thin wire mesh.  
* **1x Copper Wiring:** Used for the electro-static charge that helps pull metallic dust away from the silicates.  
* **5 units of Heat:** To soften the iron enough to be drawn into microscopic threads.

### **2\. The Fabrication Steps**

1. **Wire Drawing:** Using your **Extruder Tool** (Level 4), the Iron Ingots are pulled into wires thinner than a human hair.  
2. **Weaving:** An automated loom (part of your Level 3 Fabrication Station) weaves these threads into a cross-hatched pattern.  
3. **Electro-Charging:** The Copper Wiring is coiled around the frame. When powered, it creates a magnetic field that prevents the filter from "clogging" with iron dust while letting the silicate sand pass through.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Fine Mesh Filter isn't a standalone tool; it is a **Sub-Component**. You will need it to craft:

* **Level 3 Basic Silicates:** (The filtered output of Raw Regolith).  
* **Level 14 Oxygen Scrubbers:** (Using the mesh to trap CO2 molecules).  
* **Level 20 Automated Sifter:** (A permanent unit that uses 4 of these filters to process ore at 5x speed).

---

## **Black Box Recovery & Wear**

Because this is a physical filter constantly bombarded by abrasive space rocks:

* **Wear and Tear:** If installed on a **Permanent Sorter Unit**, the filter has a durability rating. Once it hits 0%, the unit stops producing Silicates until a new filter is "hot-swapped" in.  
* **Salvage:** If an expendable drone carrying a filter is destroyed, the **Black Box** recovery will usually return **1x Scrap Metal**, as the delicate mesh is the first thing to vaporize in an explosion.

Does the "clogging" mechanic sound like a fun challenge for the player to manage, or should the filters just work perfectly until they break?

The **Forge Logic Chip** (Level 5\) serves as the "brain" for your early-tier industrial automation. While basic drones just follow simple "move and mine" commands, the Forge Logic Chip allows a unit to understand thermal thresholds and pressure regulation.

Without this chip, your smelting process is prone to overheating, which can destroy your permanent fabrication stations.

---

## **Forge Logic Chip Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Basic Silicates:** (Level 3\) Refined from filtered regolith to create the semi-conductive base.  
* **1x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) To etch the circuitry paths onto the silicate substrate.  
* **1x Iron Ingot:** (Level 2\) To create the protective "heat shield" casing for the chip.  
* **8 units of Energy:** Required for the precision etching process.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Substrate Slicing:** A **Level 3 Fine Mesh Filter** is used to ensure the silicates are free of impurities before they are melted into a thin wafer.  
2. **Circuit Etching:** The **Level 4 Extruder Tool** is fitted with a precision tip to "print" the copper wiring onto the silicate wafer in a logic-gate pattern.  
3. **Encapsulation:** The chip is sealed inside a thin Iron casing to protect it from the extreme infrared radiation found inside forge environments.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Forge Logic Chip is the primary component for mid-tier drone intelligence and heavy industry:

* **Level 5 Steel Plating:** Required to manage the carbon-injection timing during the iron-to-steel transition.  
* **Level 10 Industrial Drill Bit:** Controls the "pulse" of the drill to prevent the bit from shattering against high-density asteroid cores.  
* **Level 13 Circuit Boards:** You will eventually combine four Forge Logic Chips with Gold Contactors to create these higher-level brains.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Overclocking"**

Since you are using a mix of **Expendable** and **Permanent** drones:

* **Permanent Units:** The Forge Logic Chip runs at 100% efficiency, keeping the forge stable and safe.  
* **Expendable Units:** You can "Overclock" the chip. This increases smelting speed by 50% but adds a **5% chance per minute** that the chip will fry, turning the drone into a Level 1 Scrap wreck.

**Logistics Tip:** If you're low on Copper, you can salvage Forge Logic Chips from wrecked Level 5 drones using a **Black Box Recovery** kit, though there is a 30% chance the chip's internal wiring is too damaged to reuse.

Would you like the player to be able to "Program" these chips with different behaviors, or should they have fixed stats once crafted?

The **Chemical Mixer** (Level 6\) is your first major step into **Fluid Dynamics and Volatile Chemistry**. While previous levels focused on solids (rocks and metal), the Chemical Mixer allows your drones to combine unstable elements into high-energy fuels.

This is a **Permanent Utility Module** that can be attached to a station or integrated into a heavy-duty drone.

---

## **Chemical Mixer Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **4x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) To create a corrosion-resistant pressurized tank.  
* **2x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9 \- *Early Unlock*) Used for the high-speed rotating impellers that stir the chemicals.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) To monitor the "Exothermic Threshold"—if the mix gets too hot, the chip triggers an emergency vent to prevent an explosion.  
* **2x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) For the internal heating elements and sensors.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Chamber Casting:** The Steel Plating is welded into a reinforced cylinder capable of handling 500 atmospheres of pressure.  
2. **Impeller Fitting:** The Hydraulics are reconfigured into a central spindle with blades designed to shear through thick molecular slurries.  
3. **Sensor Integration:** The Forge Logic Chip is hard-wired to the internal thermometer and the Copper heating coils, allowing for precise temperature control during "cooking."

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Chemical Mixer is a "Bottle-Neck" component. You cannot advance your propulsion tech without it. It is required to craft:

* **Level 6 Solid Fuel Pellets:** Compressing Carbon and Sulfur into stable blocks.  
* **Level 7 Hydrazine Propellant:** The refined liquid fuel that allows your drones to travel to distant asteroid belts.  
* **Level 17 Battery Cells:** Mixing the acidic electrolytes needed for energy storage.

---

## **Gameplay Mechanic: "Volatile Sludge"**

Because the Chemical Mixer deals with reactive substances, it introduces a new risk/reward element to your automated fleet:

* **The "Dirty" Batch:** If your **Fine Mesh Filters** are worn out, impurities can enter the mixer. This creates "Dirty Fuel," which gives your drones a 10% speed boost but causes a constant 1% durability drain.  
* **Expendable Use:** You can load a Chemical Mixer onto an **Expendable "Firefly" Drone**. If the drone is set to self-destruct, the Mixer acts as a force-multiplier, causing a massive chemical explosion that can shatter even the largest Level 10 Asteroids instantly.

**Black Box Note:** If a Chemical Mixer explodes, it is **unrecoverable**. Unlike the drill bits or plating, the mixer and its contents are usually vaporized, leaving nothing behind but "Toxic Gas" clouds that your drones must avoid for a few minutes.

Are you planning to have different "Grades" of chemicals (e.g., Grade A vs. Grade C fuel), or is it a simple "has fuel/doesn't have fuel" system?

The **Pressure Chamber** (Level 8\) is a foundational utility used to compress materials and forge components that must withstand the vacuum of space or the crushing depths of gas giants. While earlier levels rely on open-air smelting, the Pressure Chamber allows for **Atmospheric Synthesis**.

---

## **Pressure Chamber Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **4x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) Heavily reinforced to prevent catastrophic hull failure.  
* **2x Reinforced Glass:** (Level 8\) For visual monitoring of the compression process.  
* **1x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9 — *Early Unlock or Salvaged*) To power the heavy compression pistons.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) To regulate PSI levels and prevent the chamber from exploding.  
* **12 units of Energy:** Necessary to activate the hydraulic press.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Hull Forging:** The Steel Plating is welded into a double-thick spherical shell, the strongest shape for containing pressure.  
2. **Piston Integration:** The Hydraulics are mounted at the top of the dome, providing the physical force needed to crush raw materials into denser forms.  
3. **Visual Porting:** The Reinforced Glass is inset with lead seals, creating a safe observation window.  
4. **Calibration:** The Forge Logic Chip is synced to the internal pressure sensors to ensure the "Auto-Vent" triggers if the internal pressure exceeds $50,000\\text{ PSI}$.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Pressure Chamber is a "Machine Component." You must have one active in your base or on a drone to craft:

* **Level 8 Reinforced Glass:** Ironically, you need a pressure chamber to forge more high-grade glass.  
* **Level 18 Tungsten Carbide:** The only way to bond tungsten and carbon into a drill-strength alloy.  
* **Level 28 Carbon Nanotubes:** Molecular compression of carbon fibers.  
* **Level 31 Deuterium Fuel:** Compressing heavy water to extract the necessary isotopes.

---

## **Gameplay Mechanic: "The Integrity Check"**

Since this unit is under constant stress, it introduces a maintenance loop:

* **Stress Fractures:** Every 10 uses, there is a **15% chance** a stress fracture appears. If not repaired with 1x Steel Plating, the chamber has a chance to implode, destroying the drone and all nearby units.  
* **Expendable "Depth Charge":** You can load a pressurized chamber onto an **Expendable "Slammer" Drone**. By intentionally over-pressurizing it and crashing into an asteroid, you create a physical shockwave that "cracks" Level 3+ asteroids, making them easier to mine.

**Black Box Note:** In the event of an implosion, the **Forge Logic Chip** is almost always crushed, but the **Reinforced Glass** and **Hydraulics** can often be recovered from the wreckage since they are built to survive high-pressure environments.

Would you like the pressure chamber to be a standalone drone, or a module that must be attached to a larger "Mother-Drone"?

The **Fuel Synth Module** (Level 7\) is an advanced evolution of the Chemical Mixer. While the mixer simply stirs ingredients together, the **Synth Module** uses catalytic reactions to fundamentally change the molecular structure of raw gases (like Ammonia) into high-energy **Hydrazine**.

This is typically a **Permanent Module** installed on specialized "Tanker" drones or orbital refineries to support long-range fleet operations.

---

## **Fuel Synth Module Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Chemical Mixer:** (Level 6\) The core housing and agitation system.  
* **2x Reinforced Glass:** (Level 8 — *Early Unlock*) Used for high-pressure viewing ports and laser-catalyst chambers.  
* **3x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) For the exterior blast-shielding.  
* **1x Platinum Catalyst:** (Rare drop from Tier 1 Asteroids) A microscopic coating required to trigger the chemical synthesis.  
* **15 units of Energy:** Synthesis is an energy-intensive process compared to simple mixing.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Catalytic Coating:** The **Platinum** is vaporized and deposited onto the internal steel vanes of the Chemical Mixer using a **Plasma Torch** (or a high-heat forge).  
2. **Pressure Sealing:** The **Reinforced Glass** is fitted into the top of the chamber, allowing the **Forge Logic Chip** to use light-sensors to monitor the color of the reaction (which indicates fuel purity).  
3. **Synthesis Calibration:** The unit is pressurized and "primed" with a small amount of starter fuel to ensure the reaction becomes self-sustaining.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Fuel Synth Module is the heart of your "Gas Economy." It is essential for:

* **Level 7 Hydrazine Propellant:** The standard fuel for all Tier 2 and Tier 3 drones.  
* **Level 25 Cryogenic Tanks:** Managing the extreme temperatures required to keep synthesized fuel in a liquid state.  
* **Level 31 Deuterium Fuel:** Later upgraded versions of this module can "sift" heavy water molecules to create fusion fuel.

---

## **Gameplay Mechanic: "The Catalyst Decay"**

Because this module relies on a chemical reaction, it introduces a unique management layer:

* **Catalyst Poisoning:** Over time (or if using "Dirty" inputs), the Platinum coating wears off. Efficiency will drop from 100% down to 20%.  
* **The "Re-Prime" Task:** To fix it, the player must send a maintenance drone to "Re-Prime" the module with a fresh Platinum Catalyst, or the drones' travel range will be severely throttled.  
* **Expendable Strategy:** You can over-pressurize a Fuel Synth Module on an **Expendable "Breacher" Drone**. When it hits an asteroid, it doesn't just drill—it creates a "fuel-air" explosion that clears out all Level 1 surface regolith in a wide radius, leaving only the Level 2+ ore veins exposed.

**Black Box Recovery:** If a tanker drone carrying this module is destroyed, the **Black Box** can almost always recover the **Reinforced Glass** (since it's shatter-resistant) and 25% of the **Platinum**, which is the most expensive part of the build.

Would you like the synthesis process to be instant, or should it take "Real Time" to fill up a drone's fuel tank?

The **Permanent "Loader" Arm** (Level 9\) is a specialized logistical unit. Unlike your "Dart" drones that focus on retrieval, the Loader Arm is a high-torque mechanical limb designed to manipulate heavy components, swap out modules, and feed raw materials into your fabrication stations.

In your drone economy, this is a **Permanent Unit** because of its precision; it’s too expensive to treat as a one-shot tool.

---

## **Permanent "Loader" Arm Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **3x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) Forms the rugged chassis and the "bones" of the arm.  
* **2x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9\) One for the shoulder pivot and one for the gripping claw.  
* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19 — *Early Unlock or Salvaged*) Integrated into the "fingertips" to provide a magnetic grip on metallic ores.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) Programs the "Spatial Awareness" needed to move heavy objects without crushing the base or other drones.  
* **1x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) Connects the logic chip to the hydraulic actuators.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Chassis Casting:** The Steel Plating is shaped into a telescopic housing that allows the arm to extend and retract.  
2. **Hydraulic Priming:** The Hydraulics are filled with mineral oil and sealed. They are mounted at the primary joints to provide the "lifting" force.  
3. **Magnetic Tuning:** The Electromagnetic Coils are wired into the pincer claw, allowing the arm to "stick" to iron and nickel ingots for more stable transport.  
4. **Neural Calibration:** The Forge Logic Chip is flashed with a "Precision Handling" firmware, enabling the arm to handle delicate items like **Reinforced Glass** without shattering them.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Loader Arm is the backbone of your mid-game automation. It is required to:

* **Automate Smelting:** Automatically moves Raw Regolith from a storage bin into a **Solar Smelter**.  
* **Drone Repair:** Required at a Level 13 Hangar to swap out damaged **Fine Mesh Filters** or **Logic Chips**on your veteran drones.  
* **Heavy Lifting:** Moves Level 25 **Cryogenic Tanks** and Level 32 **Fusion Cores**, which are too heavy for standard Scavenger drones to carry.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Reach Factor"**

Because this is a permanent fixture or a heavy-drone attachment, its efficiency depends on placement:

* **Chain Logistics:** Players can set up a "Daisy Chain" of Loader Arms to move resources across a base without using fuel-consuming drones.  
* **Maintenance:** Since it is a **Permanent** unit, the joints will occasionally lock up if not lubricated. A locked Loader Arm stops the entire production line until it is serviced.  
* **Black Box Recovery:** If the Loader Arm is destroyed (e.g., during an asteroid impact), the **Electromagnetic Coils** are usually the only parts salvaged, as the hydraulics tend to burst under the stress of an explosion.

**Logistics Tip:** Grouping three Loader Arms around a single **Automated Sifter** (Level 20\) creates a "High-Speed Processing Hub," increasing your resource throughput by 300%.

Would you like these arms to be stationary base-builders, or should they be able to mount onto "Truck" drones to follow your fleet?

The **Expendable "Borer" Unit** (Level 10\) is your first "fire-and-forget" precision mining tool. While the basic "Dart" drones smash the surface, the Borer is designed to penetrate the hard crust of an asteroid, deploy its payload deep inside, and self-destruct to shatter the core into collectable chunks.

---

## **Expendable "Borer" Unit Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Industrial Drill Bit:** (Level 10\) The reinforced tip made of hardened steel and nickel.  
* **1x Solid Fuel Pellet:** (Level 6\) To provide the high-velocity kinetic thrust needed for penetration.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) To calculate the "Impact Vector"—ensuring it hits a fault line in the rock rather than a glancing blow.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) Minimal aerodynamic casing (since it's meant to be destroyed).  
* **5 units of Energy:** To prime the ignition sequence.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Kinetic Mounting:** The **Solid Fuel Pellet** is housed in a rear combustion chamber, essentially turning the unit into a guided missile.  
2. **Bit Alignment:** The **Industrial Drill Bit** is locked into the front nose-cone using a high-tension clamp that releases upon impact.  
3. **Core Logic:** The **Forge Logic Chip** is wired to a proximity sensor. Its only job is to detect when the unit has reached the center of the asteroid and trigger the final "overload" of the fuel cells.  
4. **Casing Weld:** The **Steel Plating** is spot-welded around the components. It doesn't need to be pretty; it just needs to hold together for one flight.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Borer is the "key" to unlocking Tier 2 materials. It is required to:

* **Harvest Tier 2 Ores:** Used to crack open asteroids containing **Lead** (Level 11\) and **Lithium** (Level 14/17).  
* **Deep-Core Mining:** Standard Scavengers can only get the top 10% of an asteroid's mass; the Borer unlocks the remaining 90%.  
* **Pathfinding:** Can be used to clear debris paths for your larger, permanent "Loader" drones.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Shatter Yield"**

Using an expendable Borer isn't just about destruction; it's about efficiency:

* **Perfect Hit:** If the Forge Logic Chip is high-quality, the asteroid shatters into large, clean chunks.  
* **Miss-Fire:** If the chip is damaged or "Overclocked," the Borer might explode prematurely, vaporizing 50% of the ore into useless dust.  
* **The "Black Box" Loop:** Since the Borer is **Expendable**, it is designed to be lost. However, if you have a **Scavenger Drone** nearby, you can recover the **Industrial Drill Bit** (50% chance) from the debris to reuse in your next Borer.

**Logistics Tip:** Don't waste Borers on small Level 1 asteroids. Save them for "Colossus" class rocks where the resource density justifies the cost of the Logic Chip.

Since this unit is a "suicide" drone, do you want the player to manually aim the impact, or should the drones be fully autonomous once they are launched?

The **Permanent "Shield" Drone** (Level 11\) marks the transition into **Tier 2: Orbital Infrastructure**. As your fleet ventures into high-radiation zones or areas with micro-meteorite storms, your delicate permanent units (like Loader Arms or Sifters) become vulnerable.

The Shield Drone doesn't mine; it acts as a bodyguard, using physical mass and magnetic fields to deflect incoming damage.

---

## **Permanent "Shield" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **10x Lead Shielding:** (Level 11\) The primary cost. This heavy plating is layered to absorb cosmic rays and kinetic impacts.  
* **4x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) The structural skeleton that holds the heavy lead slabs.  
* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19 — *Early Unlock or Salvaged*) Used to generate a "Magnetic Cushion" that slows down incoming metallic debris before it hits the hull.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13 — *Early Unlock or Salvaged*) A more advanced brain than the Forge Chip, allowing the drone to calculate "Intercept Trajectories" for incoming rocks.  
* **1x Hydrazine Propellant:** (Level 7\) To power the high-torque thrusters needed to move such a heavy, lead-filled unit.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Lead Casting:** The **Lead Shielding** is smelted into curved interlocking plates.  
2. **Core Housing:** The **Circuit Board** is placed in the absolute center of the drone, surrounded by the **Steel Plating** for maximum protection.  
3. **Coil Calibration:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are placed on the outer rim to create a 360-degree magnetic field.  
4. **Propulsion Rigging:** Because the drone is incredibly dense, the **Hydrazine** thrusters are calibrated for "Short-Burst Maneuvering" rather than long-distance travel.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Shield Drone is a "Passive Protector." Its presence in a sector provides several buffs:

* **Fleet Preservation:** Reduces the "Durability Decay" of all nearby drones by 40%.  
* **Radiation Resistance:** Allows your fleet to mine near pulsars or solar flares where unshielded drones would have their logic chips fried instantly.  
* **Mobile Cover:** You can park a Shield Drone in front of a **Permanent "Loader" Arm** to protect it while it works on a volatile asteroid.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Ablative Armor"**

Since this is a **Permanent** unit, it doesn't just "break" immediately—it degrades:

* **Lead Depletion:** As the drone takes hits, the Lead Shielding is physically stripped away. Once the "Shield Integrity" hits 0%, the drone becomes a standard **Steel Plating** chassis and loses its radiation resistance.  
* **The "Black Box" Guarantee:** Shield Drones are built to be tanks. If one is destroyed, its **Black Box** is 100% recoverable, and you can usually salvage 50% of the **Lead** from the wreck.  
* **Passive Mode:** You can set the drone to "Anchor Mode," where it shuts down its thrusters to save fuel and becomes a stationary defensive turret.

**Logistics Tip:** Don't send Shield Drones out alone. They move slowly. Always tether them to a **Permanent "Tug" Drone** (Level 29\) to move them between asteroid belts efficiently.

Since these drones are essentially "Heavy Tanks," would you like them to have a small point-defense laser to shoot down small rocks, or should they strictly be "soak-the-damage" units?

In your space-based economy, **Argon Gas** (Level 12\) isn't "crafted" from ores—it is **extracted** from the thin atmospheres of specific gas-rich asteroids or harvested from planetary exospheres. To get it, you must transition from mining solids to siphoning fluids.

This requires a **Permanent "Siphon" Drone** or a stationary **Atmospheric Condenser** module.

---

## **Argon Gas Extraction Recipe**

### **1\. Required Resources (To Process 1 Unit)**

* **50 units of "Raw Gas Vapors":** Collected by a siphon drone from "Cloudy" Asteroid variants or Gas Giant fringes.  
* **1x Cryogenic Tank:** (Level 25 — *Early Unlock or Salvaged*) To store the gas in a liquid state for transport.  
* **1x Fine Mesh Filter:** (Level 3\) To remove micro-dust particles from the intake stream.  
* **20 units of Energy:** To power the high-pressure cooling fans.

### **2\. The Extraction Process**

1. **Siphoning:** The drone uses a vacuum intake to pull in raw vapors.  
2. **Fractional Distillation:** The **Atmospheric Condenser** (a base module) cools the vapors. Since every gas has a different boiling point, Argon is separated from Oxygen and Nitrogen by lowering the temperature to exactly **\-185.8°C**.  
3. **Liquefaction:** The purified Argon is compressed into the **Cryogenic Tank**.

---

## **Functional Usage**

Argon is an inert gas, making it the perfect "Shield" for high-tech manufacturing where oxygen would cause fire or oxidation.

* **Level 12 Silicon Wafers:** Used as a "Shielding Atmosphere" during the slicing process to prevent the silicon from reacting with the air.  
* **Level 23 Excimer Lasers:** Argon is used as the medium to create the ultraviolet laser beam.  
* **Level 33 Ion Thrusters:** Argon (or Xenon) serves as the "Propellant Mass" that is ionized and shot out the back of the engine.

---

## **Gameplay Mechanic: "The Tank Loop"**

Unlike metal ingots, Argon requires a container:

* **Empty Tank Return:** When a recipe uses Argon, the **Cryogenic Tank** is returned to your inventory as an **Empty Tank**. You must send it back to the siphon station to be refilled.  
* **Volatile Storage:** If a drone carrying Argon Gas is hit by a meteorite, the tank may rupture. This creates a "Flash Freeze" cloud that disables the thrusters of any nearby drones for 30 seconds.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Gas Prospecting"**

Since you are using **Automated Drones**:

* **Scout Priority:** You should set your **Scouts** to look for "Blue-Haze" asteroids. These are rich in noble gases.  
* **Expendable "Siphon" Darts:** You can create cheap, expendable drones that fly into a gas cloud, fill up, and then "crash" back into your refinery's collection net to save on return-trip fuel.

**Logistics Tip:** Argon is the "Gatekeeper" to electronics. If your Argon supply stops, you can't build **Silicon Wafers**, which means you can't build **Circuit Boards**, which means you can't build more **Permanent Drones**. Protect your Siphon Drones at all costs\!

Would you like the gas clouds to be "infinite" resource nodes, or should they dissipate as the player harvests them?

The **Filter Frame** (Level 14\) is a structural sub-component designed to house delicate filtration media under high-pressure or high-velocity conditions. While Tier 1 used basic mesh, Tier 2 requires a rigid, vibration-resistant housing to support the air and fuel purification needs of permanent orbital structures.

---

## **Filter Frame Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) To provide the rigid outer "skeleton" of the frame.  
* **1x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) Used for the internal grounding and to power the "Anti-Clog" vibration motor.  
* **1x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9\) Specifically the seals and tensioners that lock the frame into a drone's intake manifold.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) Monitors the pressure differential; it tells the system when the filter inside the frame is full.  
* **6 units of Energy:** For the automated welding and assembly.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Precision Milling:** The **Steel Plating** is cut into a high-surface-area lattice or honeycomb pattern.  
2. **Hydraulic Seal Fitting:** The **Hydraulic** seals are fitted around the perimeter, ensuring that no gas or liquid "leaks" around the edges of the filter.  
3. **Sensor Wiring:** The **Copper Wiring** is threaded through the frame to connect the **Forge Logic Chip** to the pressure sensors.  
4. **Magnetization:** A quick electromagnetic pulse is sent through the frame to give it a slight static charge, which helps "catch" microscopic dust before it even hits the mesh.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Filter Frame is a "Carrier" component. It doesn't do much on its own, but it is the required housing for:

* **Level 14 Oxygen Scrubbers:** Holds the lithium-hydroxide sheets that clean the air in permanent habitats.  
* **Level 20 Automated Sifter:** The frame holds the **Fine Mesh Filters** in place against the heavy vibration of the ore-shaking mechanism.  
* **Level 7 Fuel Synth Module:** (Upgraded version) Advanced modules use these frames to hold the platinum catalysts in the path of the ammonia flow.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Hot-Swapping"**

In an automated drone fleet, the Filter Frame is designed for longevity, but the *contents* are not:

* **The "Cassette" System:** Drones equipped with Filter Frames can be serviced in flight. A **Loader Arm**(Level 9\) can pull out a dirty filter and slide a fresh one into the Frame in seconds, without needing to disassemble the drone.  
* **Structural Failure:** If a Filter Frame takes direct kinetic damage, it warps. A warped frame cannot be "Hot-Swapped," forcing the drone to return to a **Permanent Repair Hangar** for a full hull replacement.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

Because the frame is essentially a reinforced steel box:

* **High Salvage Rate:** If a drone explodes, the Filter Frame has an **80% recovery rate**.  
* **Black Box Data:** The Forge Logic Chip inside the frame often records the "Pre-Impact Contamination Levels," which can give the player a bonus to their **Scouting Data** for that specific asteroid belt.

**Logistics Tip:** Always keep a stockpile of 5-10 Filter Frames. They are the "wear-and-tear" items of Tier 2; without them, your life support and sifting operations will eventually grind to a halt due to dust contamination.

Since these frames hold the filters for Oxygen Scrubbers, do you want your permanent space stations to have a "Breathable Air" meter that players have to manage?

The **Silver Contact** (Level 15\) is a high-conductivity component essential for the transition into Tier 2 energy systems. While copper is great for basic wiring, silver provides the near-zero resistance needed for high-efficiency **Solar Cell Sheets** and precision electronics.

---

## **Silver Contact Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Silver Ore:** Mined from "Noble" or "Metallic" asteroid variants using **Expendable "Borer" Units** (Level 10).  
* **1x Extruder Tool:** (Level 4\) Used to pull the silver into ultra-fine conductive ribbons.  
* **1x Argon Gas:** (Level 12\) Used as a shielding atmosphere to prevent the silver from tarnishing or oxidizing during the melting process.  
* **10 units of Heat:** Required to reach the melting point of silver ($961.8\\text{°C}$).

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Noble Smelting:** The Silver Ore is placed in a vacuum-sealed crucible flooded with **Argon Gas**. This ensures the silver remains at "Five Nines" (99.999%) purity.  
2. **Ribbon Drawing:** The **Extruder Tool** draws the molten silver into flat, paper-thin ribbons rather than round wires. This increases the surface area for electrical contact.  
3. **Flash Cooling:** The ribbons are rapidly cooled to lock in their molecular structure, preventing the formation of large crystals that would increase electrical resistance.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Silver Contact is the "Efficiency Engine" of your fleet. It is a core requirement for:

* **Level 15 Solar Cell Sheets:** These contacts collect the electrons knocked loose by sunlight and funnel them into the battery.  
* **Level 22 Gold Contactors:** (Level 22\) High-tier electronics use Silver Contacts as a base layer before applying gold plating for corrosion resistance.  
* **Level 17 Battery Cells:** Used for the internal terminals to ensure rapid charging and discharging without heat buildup.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Energy Throughput"**

Integrating silver into your automated systems changes how your energy behaves:

* **The "Cool Run" Bonus:** Units equipped with Silver Contacts generate **15% less heat** during operation. This is critical for drones working near sun-facing asteroid sides.  
* **Degradation:** Silver is softer than copper or steel. If a drone takes heavy vibration damage (e.g., from a **Sonic Resonator**), there is a chance the Silver Contacts will "crack," reducing the drone's energy efficiency by 50% until repaired.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Value Salvage:** Because silver is a "Noble Metal," it survives most explosions without vaporizing.  
* **Yield:** A destroyed drone will almost always yield **1x Silver Scrap**, which can be smelted back into an ingot with 0% material loss, making your silver economy very sustainable.

**Logistics Tip:** Silver is often found in the same asteroid belts as **Lead**. If you are sending **Shield Drones** out to harvest lead, equip them with an extra cargo pod to bring back Silver Ore simultaneously to maximize your fuel efficiency.

Since these are used for Solar Cells, are you planning on having "Dark Zones" (like the shadow of a planet) where solar-powered drones will shut down?

The **Heat Sink** (Level 16\) is a vital component for thermal management. In the vacuum of space, heat doesn't just "blow away" because there is no air for convection. Instead, heat must be collected and moved to **Thermal Radiators** to be beamed away as infrared light.

Without Heat Sinks, your high-performance drones (like those with lasers or heavy drills) would melt their own internal circuitry within minutes.

---

## **Heat Sink Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **5x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) Copper is used for its excellent thermal conductivity to "wick" heat away from the source.  
* **2x Aluminum Sheets:** (Level 16 — *Tier 2 Mineral*) Aluminum is used for the "fins" because it is lightweight and has a high surface area.  
* **1x Extruder Tool:** (Level 4\) To press the aluminum into ultra-thin, high-surface-area fins.  
* **1x Silver Contact:** (Level 15\) Placed at the "Thermal Interface" (where the sink touches the CPU/Motor) to ensure the fastest possible heat transfer.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Thermal Base Forging:** The **Silver Contact** is bonded to a thick block of compressed **Copper**. This creates the "Heat Spreader" that sits directly on the component.  
2. **Fin Extrusion:** The **Aluminum** is pushed through the **Extruder Tool** to create a series of thin, accordion-like fins.  
3. **Bonding:** The fins are fused to the copper base.  
4. **Vacuum Testing:** The unit is placed in a vacuum chamber to ensure there are no air pockets between the silver and copper, as even a tiny bubble of air acts as an insulator and would cause the sink to fail.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Heat Sink is a "Passive Cooling" module. It is a required sub-component for:

* **Level 16 Thermal Radiators:** The sink collects the heat; the radiator gets rid of it.  
* **Level 23 Excimer Lasers:** Lasers generate massive amounts of waste heat that must be managed to maintain beam focus.  
* **Level 32 Fusion Core:** Even advanced fusion requires massive heat-syncing to prevent the magnetic bottle from failing.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Thermal Throttling"**

In your automated drone fleet, Heat Sinks dictate the "Duty Cycle" of your equipment:

* **The Overheat Limit:** Every drone has a "Heat Capacity." Once full, the drone must stop all work to cool down. Adding more Heat Sinks increases this capacity.  
* **Permanent Unit Degradation:** If a permanent unit (like a **Loader Arm**) operates without a functional Heat Sink, its **Logic Chips** will permanently lose 1% of their processing speed every minute due to heat damage.  
* **Expendable "Overload":** You can remove the Heat Sinks from an **Expendable "Borer" Unit** to save resources. It will mine faster because it's running "hot," but it will guaranteed explode after 60 seconds of use.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Durability:** Heat Sinks are incredibly hardy. They don't have moving parts, so they rarely break.  
* **Yield:** If a drone is destroyed, the Heat Sink is almost always recoverable as **"Melted Slag."** While it can't be used as a Heat Sink anymore, it provides a high yield of **Copper** and **Aluminum** when tossed back into the Smelter.

**Logistics Tip:** If you're mining near a star, your drones will need **Double Heat Sinks** just to stay powered on. Always check the "Solar Flux" of a sector before deploying your permanent fleet.

Since space is a vacuum, would you like the "Cooling Rate" to be faster when the drone is in the shadow of an asteroid?

The **Permanent "Battery" Drone** (Level 17\) is the mobile power grid of your fleet. While Scavenger drones can return to base to recharge, your long-range mining operations require a dedicated power source that follows the fleet. These drones act as "tethers," staying near working units and beaming or docking energy to them.

---

## **Permanent "Battery" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **4x Battery Cells:** (Level 17\) The core energy storage units.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) To manage the "Smart Charge" distribution and prevent over-discharging.  
* **1x Silver Contact:** (Level 15\) For zero-resistance power transfer during fast-charging.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) To house the delicate chemical cells in a rigid chassis.  
* **1x Heat Sink:** (Level 16\) Rapidly discharging high-density energy creates massive heat; this prevents the drone from melting.  
* **10 units of Energy:** To "prime" the battery with its first charge.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Cell Sequencing:** The **Battery Cells** are wired in a series-parallel grid within the **Steel Plating** chassis.  
2. **Thermal Management:** The **Heat Sink** is bonded to the battery array using the **Silver Contact** as a thermal bridge.  
3. **Brain Installation:** The **Circuit Board** is programmed with "Load Balancing" protocols so the drone can charge multiple smaller units simultaneously.  
4. **Final Insulation:** The internals are vacuum-sealed to ensure no chemical leaks can occur if the hull is dented.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Battery Drone is a "Force Multiplier." Its presence enables:

* **Deep Space Mining:** Allows drones to operate in the "Dark Zone" of asteroids or planets where solar power is unavailable.  
* **Emergency Jump-Start:** If a **Permanent "Loader" Arm** runs out of power and freezes, the Battery Drone can dock and restart its systems.  
* **High-Power Buff:** When tethered to an **Industrial Drill Bit**, it allows the drill to "Overclock," mining 25% faster by pulling extra current.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Power Chain"**

Since you are managing an automated fleet, the Battery Drone introduces a logistics loop:

* **The "Charge Relay":** You can set your **Permanent "Battery" Drones** to cycle between a **Solar Array** (at base) and the **Mining Site**. One drone charges while the other provides power, ensuring 100% uptime.  
* **The "Explosive Risk":** Unlike other permanent drones, the Battery Drone is a "flying bomb." If its integrity hits 0% due to damage, it doesn't just stop—it triggers an **Electro-Magnetic Pulse (EMP)** that disables all nearby drones for 60 seconds.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Volatile Salvage:** Because the battery chemicals are highly reactive, an explosion usually destroys the **Battery Cells**.  
* **Yield:** However, the **Black Box** recovery almost always saves the **Circuit Board** and the **Silver Contact**, allowing you to rebuild the drone at a 40% discount on resources.

**Logistics Tip:** Pair your Battery Drone with a **Permanent "Shield" Drone** (Level 11). If the battery unit is destroyed, the Shield Drone can absorb the EMP blast, protecting the rest of your fleet from the shutdown.

Would you like these drones to use "Wireless Beaming" to charge others from a distance, or should they have to physically dock with a unit to transfer power?

The **Permanent "Sorter" Unit** (Level 20\) is the crown jewel of your Tier 2 logistics. Up until now, your drones have been dumping mixed piles of rock and metal into storage. The Sorter Unit automates the "cleanup," vibrating and magnetically pulling apart the raw materials so that your smelters receive 100% pure ore.

This is a **Permanent Utility Unit** that usually sits at the mouth of your refinery or on a dedicated "Processing Barge."

---

## **Permanent "Sorter" Unit Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **5x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) The heavy-duty frame required to withstand constant high-frequency vibration.  
* **4x Filter Frames:** (Level 14\) These house the various mesh grades used to separate rock sizes.  
* **2x Circuit Boards:** (Level 13\) One to manage the vibration frequency and one to control the magnetic "Pick-and-Place" logic.  
* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) Used to generate the magnetic fields that yank iron, nickel, and silver out of the dirt.  
* **1x Heat Sink:** (Level 16\) The vibration motors generate significant friction heat that must be bled off.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Vibration Bed Assembly:** The **Steel Plating** is configured into a multi-tiered shaking table.  
2. **Filter Integration:** The **Filter Frames** (pre-loaded with mesh) are slotted into the tiers, starting with coarse mesh at the top and fine mesh at the bottom.  
3. **Magnetic Array Wiring:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are positioned at the "output" chutes to catch metallic particles as they fall.  
4. **Logic Synchronization:** The **Circuit Boards** are synced to a "Material Scanner." This allows the Sorter to adjust its shaking speed based on whether it’s processing light silicates or heavy iron.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Sorter Unit is the "Efficiency Gate" for Tier 3\. It is used to:

* **Purify Ores:** Converts "Mixed Asteroid Debris" into 100% pure stacks of Iron, Nickel, Copper, or Silicates.  
* **Rare Element Discovery:** There is a small chance (5%) that the Sorter finds "Trace Elements" (like Gold or Titanium) that standard scavenger drones would have missed.  
* **Refinery Input:** Feeding a **Solar Smelter** from a Sorter Unit reduces smelting time by 20% because the smelter isn't wasting energy on "junk" rock.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Resonance Frequency"**

Managing a Sorter requires keeping an eye on its settings:

* **The "Sweet Spot":** Each material has a resonance frequency. If the player sets the Sorter correctly, yield increases. If set incorrectly, the Sorter might "shatter" delicate materials (like **Argon Gas** canisters or **Reinforced Glass**), destroying them.  
* **Maintenance:** Because it is a permanent unit that vibrates, the **Steel Plating** will eventually develop "stress cracks." If it hits 0% durability, it will literally shake itself apart into Level 1 Scrap.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Structural Survival:** Because the unit is built to handle vibration, it is very sturdy.  
* **Yield:** If destroyed by an outside force (like an asteroid impact), you can usually recover the **Electromagnetic Coils** and at least 2 of the **Filter Frames** intact. The **Circuit Boards**, however, are usually fried by the mechanical trauma.

**Logistics Tip:** Place your **Permanent "Loader" Arm** (Level 9\) directly next to the Sorter. The Arm can pull the purified ingots off the Sorter and place them directly into your **Permanent "Battery" Drone's** charging dock or a storage crate.

Would you like the Sorter to handle one material at a time, or should it be able to split a mixed pile into four different crates simultaneously?

The **Arc Welder** (Level 21\) marks your entry into **Tier 3: Precision Engineering**. While Tier 1 and 2 relied on basic mechanical fasteners and spot-welding, the Arc Welder uses high-voltage electricity to fuse high-density metals like Titanium.

This is a **Permanent Tool Attachment** usually mounted on a specialized construction drone or a fixed fabrication arm.

---

## **Arc Welder Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) To generate the high-intensity electric arc.  
* **1x Battery Cell:** (Level 17\) To provide the rapid discharge of current needed to jump-start the arc.  
* **1x Tungsten Carbide:** (Level 18\) Used for the non-consumable electrode tip because of its extreme melting point.  
* **2x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) Heavy-duty cables to handle the high amperage.  
* **1x Argon Gas:** (Level 12\) Critical for "Shielded Welding"—the gas prevents oxygen from making the weld brittle.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Electrode Housing:** The **Tungsten Carbide** is machined into a needle-point tip and housed in a heat-resistant ceramic sleeve.  
2. **Transformer Wiring:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are wired in a step-down configuration to convert high-voltage battery power into high-amperage welding power.  
3. **Gas Manifold:** A small valve is attached to the nozzle to release a steady stream of **Argon Gas** around the tungsten tip.  
4. **Circuit Integration:** The unit is connected to a drone’s power bus, ensuring the **Battery Cell** acts as a buffer to prevent power surges from frying the drone's brain.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Arc Welder is an "Advanced Assembler." It is a mandatory requirement for:

* **Level 21 Titanium Alloy:** You cannot bond titanium to steel without the heat and gas shielding of an arc welder.  
* **Level 25 Cryogenic Tanks:** To ensure the tanks are "Vacuum-Tight" so they don't leak precious gas.  
* **Permanent Repair Hangar:** This base module uses Arc Welders to fully restore the durability of your permanent drones.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Weld Integrity"**

In an automated fleet, the quality of your welding matters:

* **Gas Consumption:** The Arc Welder consumes **Argon Gas** while active. If you run out of Argon mid-weld, the "Weld Integrity" drops. A drone with low weld integrity has a 20% chance to lose a limb or plate during high-speed maneuvers.  
* **The "Bright Light" Hazard:** Arc welding creates intense UV light. If a drone without **Reinforced Glass**sensors looks directly at the arc, its optical sensors will "blind," causing it to wander aimlessly until repaired.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Durability:** The **Tungsten Carbide** tip is nearly indestructible, but the **Electromagnetic Coils** are sensitive to kinetic impact.  
* **Yield:** If a welding drone is destroyed, you are 100% guaranteed to recover the **Tungsten Carbide** tip, which is often the hardest part of the recipe to replenish.

**Logistics Tip:** Assign an **Arc-Welder Drone** to follow your **Permanent "Shield" Drones**. The welder can perform "Field Repairs" on the shield's lead plating, extending its life in high-danger zones without needing to return to base.

Would you like the welder to be able to "Deconstruct" enemy drones or old structures to get 100% of the resources back?

The **Precision Micro-Drone** (Level 22\) is the smallest autonomous unit in your fleet. Unlike the bulky "Dart" or "Borer" units, the Micro-Drone is designed for "Internal Logistics"—it flies *inside* the hulls of your larger permanent stations and drones to perform micro-repairs and component swaps.

It is a **Permanent Unit**, but due to its size, it is incredibly fragile.

---

## **Precision Micro-Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Micro-Processor:** (Level 24 — *Early Unlock*) The miniaturized "brain" required for sub-millimeter maneuvering.  
* **2x Gold Contactors:** (Level 22\) Gold is used because it doesn't oxidize and allows for perfect signal transmission at a microscopic scale.  
* **1x Silver Contact:** (Level 15\) For the high-efficiency battery terminals.  
* **1x Graphene Sheet:** (Level 34 — *Early Unlock or Rare Salvage*) To create a lightweight, "paper-thin" chassis that can still withstand high-speed flight.  
* **1x Electromagnetic Coil:** (Level 19\) Scaled down to create a "Micro-Induction" engine (no fuel required; it draws power wirelessly from the base).

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Chassis Weaving:** The **Graphene Sheet** is folded into a multi-limbed frame using a **Molecular Assembler** or a **Precision Loader Arm**.  
2. **Neural Seating:** The **Micro-Processor** is bonded to the frame using **Gold Contactors**. This ensures the drone can process 1,000 flight adjustments per second.  
3. **Engine Tuning:** The **Electromagnetic Coil** is wrapped around a central core, allowing the drone to "hover" using the magnetic field of your space station.  
4. **Optical Calibration:** The drone is fitted with a microscopic lens (made from **Reinforced Glass** scraps) to allow it to "see" cracks in solder or logic gates.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Precision Micro-Drone is the "White Blood Cell" of your fleet. It is required to:

* **Automated Maintenance:** It can repair **Circuit Boards** or **Logic Chips** while the parent drone is still flying, preventing "Permanent Degradation."  
* **Level 22 Gold Contactors:** Micro-Drones are actually required to *build* more of themselves and other Level 22+ electronics because human-sized Loader Arms are too clumsy for the task.  
* **Component Salvage:** When a drone is destroyed, Micro-Drones can be sent into the debris to recover 15% more materials than a standard Scavenger could.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Swarm Power"**

Micro-drones are weak individually but powerful in groups:

* **The "Hive" Effect:** If you have 10 Micro-Drones assigned to one **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**, they can keep its durability at 100% indefinitely, even while it's running at "Overclocked" speeds.  
* **Wireless Range:** They do not use fuel; they use **Induction Power**. If they fly too far away from a **Permanent "Battery" Drone** or your Home Base, they will simply fall dormant and float away in the vacuum.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Total Loss Risk:** Because they are so small and made of Graphene, if a Micro-Drone is hit by even a grain of space dust, it is usually vaporized.  
* **Yield:** You rarely recover anything from a destroyed Micro-Drone except for a trace amount of **Gold Scrap**.

**Logistics Tip:** Store your Micro-Drones inside the "Hangar Bay" of your **Permanent "Shield" Drones**. This keeps them safe during transit, and they can zip out to repair the shield's lead plating as soon as the battle or storm is over.

Since these drones are essentially "intelligent tools," would you like to be able to "Research" different software packages for them (e.g., a "Repair Script" vs. a "Salvage Script")?

The **Expendable "Lens" Drone** (Level 23\) is a specialized "kamikaze" optical unit. Its primary purpose isn't to mine or move cargo, but to act as a high-precision focal point for your base's stationary lasers. By flying into a dangerous zone and positioning itself perfectly, it allows you to fire powerful beams from a safe distance, using its internal lens to amplify and redirect the energy.

---

## **Expendable "Lens" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Excimer Laser:** (Level 23\) The core optical assembly that provides the initial beam-focusing logic.  
* **2x Reinforced Glass:** (Level 8\) Polished and treated to act as the primary refracting lens.  
* **1x Silver Contact:** (Level 15\) To power the high-speed gimbal motors that keep the lens steady.  
* **1x Forge Logic Chip:** (Level 5\) A basic "Brain" used to maintain a "Lock-On" coordinate provided by the base.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) The minimal casing required to protect the glass during its flight to the target.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Optical Polishing:** The **Reinforced Glass** is subjected to a high-heat "Flame-Polish" using a **Plasma Torch** to ensure there are zero microscopic scratches.  
2. **Gimbal Mounting:** The glass is mounted on a two-axis pivot powered by **Silver Contacts**, allowing the lens to tilt even if the drone is spinning.  
3. **Laser Alignment:** The **Excimer Laser** sub-component is aligned behind the glass. This ensures that when the "Master Beam" from your base hits the drone, it is focused into a needle-thin point.  
4. **Expendable Shelling:** The components are encased in a thin **Steel Plating** shell. Because the drone is designed to be destroyed by the heat of the beam it is carrying, structural longevity is not a priority.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Lens Drone is a "Force Multiplier" for your long-range mining and defense:

* **Level 23 Excimer Lasers:** You need these drones to actually *use* your base-mounted Excimer Lasers at a distance.  
* **Deep-Core Thermal Mining:** By focusing a laser through the Lens Drone, you can "melt" through Level 4 Asteroid crusts without sending a physical drill.  
* **Point Defense:** A swarm of Lens Drones can create a "Laser Web" around your base, vaporizing incoming micro-meteorites before they hit your **Permanent "Shield" Drones**.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Melt-Down"**

Because this drone is focusing massive amounts of energy through a glass lens, it has a built-in expiration date:

* **The "Focus" Timer:** Every second the drone is redirecting a laser, its "Thermal Load" increases. After 30 seconds of continuous fire, the **Reinforced Glass** will melt, and the drone will explode.  
* **The "Chain Reaction":** If you line up three Lens Drones in a row, the laser beam's power triples, but the drones will melt 3x faster.  
* **Black Box Recovery:** There is a **0% recovery rate** for a Lens Drone that has "Melted Down." The glass and steel are vaporized into a fine metallic mist.

**Logistics Tip:** Use your **Permanent "Loader" Arm** to constantly "feed" new Lens Drones into a launch tube. In a heavy mining operation, you might go through 10-20 of these "Expendable" units per hour.

Would you like the "Lens" Drones to be able to "Burn" enemy drones, or should they strictly be used for mining and defense?

The **Lithography Kit** (Level 24\) is the ultimate precision instrument of **Tier 3**. While the **Arc Welder** handles heavy fusion, the Lithography Kit uses extreme ultraviolet (EUV) light to "print" complex logic pathways onto Silicon Wafers.

This is a **Permanent Tool Attachment**. Without it, you cannot progress into high-level AI or Micro-Processors.

---

## **Lithography Kit Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Excimer Laser:** (Level 23\) To generate the high-frequency light beam required for etching.  
* **3x Expendable "Lens" Drones:** (Level 23 — *Cannibalized*) The high-grade optics from these drones are stripped to create the internal "Reduction Lens" of the kit.  
* **1x Precision Micro-Drone:** (Level 22 — *Integrated*) The micro-drone is permanently mounted inside the kit to perform real-time lens realignments during the printing process.  
* **4x Gold Contactors:** (Level 22\) To ensure the laser signals travel to the lens gimbals with zero latency.  
* **2x Argon Gas:** (Level 12\) Floods the kit’s interior to prevent a single speck of dust from ruining the wafer.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Optic Alignment:** The lenses from the **Lens Drones** are stacked in a "Vacuum Column." This focuses the **Excimer Laser** down to a width of 5 nanometers.  
2. **Micro-Drone Docking:** The **Micro-Drone** is hardwired into the chassis. It acts as the "Optical Engineer," physically shifting the lenses by microns to account for the heat expansion of the laser.  
3. **Atmospheric Sealing:** The unit is encased in a double-walled lead/steel shell and pressurized with **Argon Gas**.  
4. **Gold-Path Calibration:** The **Gold Contactors** are synced with the **Circuit Board** of the parent machine, allowing for "Sub-Millisecond" etching instructions.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Lithography Kit is a "Master Fabricator." It is the only tool capable of creating:

* **Level 24 Micro-Processors:** The advanced "brains" for Tier 4 and Tier 5 drones.  
* **Level 26 AI Core:** A processor so complex it requires three Lithography Kits working in parallel.  
* **Level 30 Stealth Plating:** Etching microscopic "light-trap" patterns onto drone hulls to make them invisible to radar.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Purity Yield"**

Using a Lithography Kit introduces a "Silicon Waste" mechanic:

* **Yield Rate:** Every time you print a **Micro-Processor**, there is a chance the wafer "fails" due to vibration or impurities.  
  * *Base Success:* 70%.  
  * *With 10 Micro-Drones Nearby:* 95%.  
* **The "Clean Room" Requirement:** The kit must be mounted on a **Permanent Station** that has at least two **Filter Frames** (Level 14\) active, or the dust will cause the Excimer Laser to "diffract," destroying the Silicon Wafer.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Extremely Fragile:** If the drone or station carrying the Lithography Kit is destroyed, the internal lenses shatter instantly.  
* **Yield:** You will **never** recover the lenses or the laser. However, you are 100% guaranteed to recover the **Gold Contactors** and the **Micro-Processor** from the integrated Micro-Drone, allowing you to start the rebuild with the most expensive "brains" intact.

**Logistics Tip:** Never put a Lithography Kit on a front-line mining drone. Keep it at your deepest, most protected base, shielded by at least two **Permanent "Shield" Drones**. It is the single most valuable tool in your mid-game arsenal.

Since this kit allows you to build **Micro-Processors**, do you want to start specializing your drone "Personalities" (e.g., making a "Aggressive Scavenger" vs. a "Cautious Miner")?

the **Cooling Unit** (Level 25\) is the active counterpart to the passive Heat Sink. While a Heat Sink simply moves heat to the surface, the Cooling Unit uses a closed-loop refrigeration cycle to aggressively drop the temperature of high-output machinery.

This is a **Permanent Utility Module** essential for maintaining "Tier 3" weapons and engines that would otherwise melt in seconds.

---

## **Cooling Unit Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Heat Sinks:** (Level 16\) Used as the "Evaporator" and "Condenser" plates within the unit.  
* **1x Cryogenic Tank (Filled):** (Level 25\) Must be filled with **Argon Gas** (Level 12\) or Liquid Nitrogen to act as the refrigerant.  
* **1x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9\) Modified to act as the compressor pump that cycles the coolant.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) To manage the "Thermal Throttle" and prevent the coolant from freezing the internal components.  
* **2x Copper Wiring:** (Level 4\) To power the high-RPM compressor motor.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Loop Integration:** The **Basic Hydraulics** pump is connected to a series of copper coils that wrap around the primary **Heat Sink**.  
2. **Coolant Charging:** The **Argon** from the **Cryogenic Tank** is injected into the loop. The system is then hermetically sealed to prevent the gas from escaping into the vacuum.  
3. **Heat Exchange Mounting:** The second **Heat Sink** is attached to the outside of the unit, acting as the "Radiator" where the collected heat is expelled.  
4. **Logic Calibration:** The **Circuit Board** is wired to thermal sensors. It is programmed to "Pulse" the pump, saving energy when the drone is idle and maxing out when the drone is firing its lasers.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Cooling Unit is a "Power Unlocker." It is a required sub-component for:

* **Level 25 Cryogenic Tanks:** Ironically, you need a Cooling Unit to keep the tanks cold enough to store liquid gases.  
* **Level 26 AI Core:** The processing density of an AI core is so high it requires dedicated active cooling to function.  
* **Level 33 Ion Thrusters:** Prevents the thruster nozzle from deforming during long-distance burns.  
* **Heavy Railguns:** Clears the heat from the rails after every shot to allow for a faster rate of fire.

![][image1]

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Thermal Overload"**

In your automated fleet, the Cooling Unit changes the "Overheat" math:

* **Sub-Zero Buff:** While active, the drone's "Heat Capacity" is effectively doubled. You can run your **Arc Welders** or **Excimer Lasers** for twice as long.  
* **The "Leak" Hazard:** If the Cooling Unit takes damage, there is a chance the pressurized coolant loop will rupture. This creates a **Cryo-Cloud** that instantly freezes the drone's own **Loader Arms** or **Gimbals**, locking them in place for 60 seconds.  
* **Energy Drain:** Unlike the passive Heat Sink, the Cooling Unit consumes **5 Energy per minute** while active. If your **Permanent "Battery" Drone** runs dry, the cooling stops, and the unit it was protecting may melt.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Fragile Internals:** The compressor pump is sensitive. If the drone explodes, the **Hydraulics** are usually destroyed.  
* **Yield:** You are 90% guaranteed to recover the two **Heat Sinks** and the **Circuit Board**. The **Cryogenic Tank** is 50% likely to be salvaged, but it will always be **Empty** upon recovery.

**Logistics Tip:** Don't put a Cooling Unit on every drone—it's too expensive. Only install them on your "Capital Drones" or stationary "Fabrication Hubs" that house your **Lithography Kits**.

Since this unit requires a filled **Cryogenic Tank**, should we prioritize the blueprint for the **Cryogenic Tank (Level 25\)** itself, or move on to the **AI Core (Level 26\)**?

The **Expendable "Cutter" Drone** (Level 26\) is the offensive evolution of your mining tech. While the "Borer" uses brute force to shatter rock, the Cutter uses a high-frequency vibration blade to slice through the "Super-Alloys" found in Tier 3 debris and derelict ship hulls.

It is designed for one job: precision dismantling. Once its blade dulls or the drone is compromised, it is programmed to "over-rev" its motor, turning its own chassis into a final kinetic impactor.

---

## **Expendable "Cutter" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Tungsten Carbide:** (Level 18\) Machined into a serrated, high-heat resistant circular saw or vibrating blade.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) To prevent the blade motor from melting during high-friction cuts.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) To calculate "Structural Weak Points" so the drone knows exactly where to cut to make a hull collapse.  
* **1x Hydrazine Propellant:** (Level 7\) For the high-speed "Dash" maneuvers needed to avoid defensive turrets.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) The minimalist frame.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Blade Tempering:** The **Tungsten Carbide** is sharpened to a molecular edge using an **Arc Welder**.  
2. **Thermal Seating:** The **Cooling Unit** is wrapped directly around the motor housing. This allows the blade to spin at 50,000 RPM without seizing.  
3. **Vibration Dampening:** The **Circuit Board** is mounted on a "Floating" sub-frame to protect it from the intense tremors of the cutting blade.  
4. **Fuel Injection:** The **Hydrazine** is loaded into a single-use booster, giving the drone enough speed to "lunge" at its target.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Cutter is your "Skeleton Key" for Tier 3 environments. It is used to:

* **Salvage Derelict Hulls:** The only way to harvest **Titanium Alloy** (Level 21\) from old space stations.  
* **Precision Sabotage:** If an asteroid is too large for a Borer, a swarm of Cutters can "carve" it into manageable pieces for your **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**.  
* **Combat Role:** It can slice through the **Lead Shielding** (Level 11\) of hostile units, exposing their **Circuit Boards** to your lasers.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Blade Durability"**

Unlike lasers, the Cutter is a physical tool subject to friction:

* **Friction Heat:** Even with a **Cooling Unit**, the blade will eventually lose its "Bite." After 2 minutes of continuous cutting, the drone's efficiency drops by 80%.  
* **The "Final Serration":** When the blade is about to break, the drone performs a **"Core Breach"**maneuver. It rams its remaining Tungsten blade into the target and detonates its Hydrazine fuel, creating a localized explosion.  
* **Black Box Recovery:** Because the drone "Core Breaches" at the end of its life, the **Recovery Rate is 0%**. This is a pure resource-sink drone.

---

## **Gameplay Comparison: Borer vs. Cutter**

| Feature | Expendable Borer (Lvl 10\) | Expendable Cutter (Lvl 26\) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Damage Type** | Kinetic (Shatter) | Thermal/Mechanical (Slice) |
| **Best Target** | Rock/Brittle Ore | Alloys/Refined Metals |
| **Resource Cost** | Low (Steel/Fuel) | High (Tungsten/Cooling) |
| **Salvage Potential** | 50% (Drill Bit) | 0% (Total Destruction) |

**Logistics Tip:** Don't waste Cutters on raw asteroids. They are far too expensive. Keep them in your **Permanent "Shield" Drone's** cargo bay and only launch them when you encounter "Armored" resource nodes or derelict tech.

Since the Cutter is expensive and has a 0% salvage rate, do you want to add a "Blade Sharpening Station" module to your base that allows them to return and "Refurbish" instead of exploding?

The **Sub-Zero Chamber** (Level 27\) is the cryo-engineering evolution of the Level 8 Pressure Chamber. While the earlier version focused on physical compression, the Sub-Zero Chamber focuses on **Molecular Stabilization**. It is a **Permanent Utility Unit** used to forge materials that are too volatile to exist at room temperature.

---

## **Sub-Zero Chamber Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Pressure Chamber:** (Level 8\) Acts as the structural housing. It must be reinforced to handle the contraction of freezing metals.  
* **2x Cooling Units:** (Level 25\) Mounted in a "Cascading" configuration to reach temperatures near Absolute Zero ($0\\text{ K}$ or $-273.15\\text{°C}$).  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26 — *Early Unlock*) To manage the hyper-complex thermal sensors; a standard Circuit Board would "lag" and allow the chamber to warm up, ruining the batch.  
* **2x Cryogenic Tanks (Filled):** (Level 25\) Used as the initial "Heat Sink" to drop the temperature before the active cooling takes over.  
* **4x Lead Shielding:** (Level 11\) To insulate the chamber from external solar radiation.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Thermal Isolation:** The **Pressure Chamber** is lined with **Lead Shielding**. A vacuum gap is created between the layers to prevent heat transfer.  
2. **Coolant Cascading:** The two **Cooling Units** are wired together. The first unit cools the second, allowing the second unit to reach temperatures far below standard refrigeration limits.  
3. **Sensor Calibration:** The **AI Core** is installed. It must be programmed to predict "Thermal Spikes" from the external environment and adjust the cooling flow in nanoseconds.  
4. **Argon Purge:** The internal chamber is flushed with **Argon Gas** (Level 12\) to remove all moisture, preventing "Ice Spikes" from forming and puncturing the delicate materials inside.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Sub-Zero Chamber is a "Material Transmuter." It is the only unit capable of crafting:

* **Level 28 Superconductors:** Forging **Silver Contacts** and **Copper** at near-zero temperatures to eliminate electrical resistance.  
* **Level 31 Deuterium Fuel:** Stabilizing the heavy hydrogen isotopes extracted from gas giants.  
* **Level 35 Quantum Chips:** The next tier of processing, which can only be etched in a perfectly cold environment.  
* **Bio-Stasis Pods:** If your project involves organic "Pilots" or biological samples, this chamber is the base for their life-support.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Cold Snap"**

Operating at these temperatures introduces a new risk/reward loop:

* **Material Brittleness:** While the chamber is active, its **Steel Plating** becomes as brittle as glass. A single micro-meteorite impact that would normally dent a drone will instead cause the entire Sub-Zero Chamber to **shatter**.  
* **Power Hunger:** This is your most energy-expensive unit. It requires a dedicated **Permanent "Battery" Drone** (Level 17\) just to stay in "Standby Mode."  
* **The "Flash Freeze" Salvage:** If the chamber is destroyed while processing, it releases a "Thermal Vacuum." This instantly freezes any nearby **Expendable Drones**, turning them into frozen projectiles that can be recovered but are temporarily non-functional.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Internal Integrity:** Because of the **AI Core's** predictive shielding, the "Brain" of the unit almost always survives an explosion.
