* **Yield:** You are 100% guaranteed to recover the **AI Core**. However, the **Cooling Units** and **Cryogenic Tanks** are usually lost due to the rapid thermal expansion during a breach.

**Logistics Tip:** Place your Sub-Zero Chamber in the "Permanent Shadow" of a large moon or asteroid. Reducing the "Ambient Heat" of the environment will lower the unit's energy consumption by 30%.

Now that you have the ability to stabilize **Superconductors**, would you like to explore the recipe for the **Superconductor (Level 28\)**, or focus on the **Quantum Chip (Level 35\)** to upgrade your AI capabilities?

The **Molecular Press** (Level 28\) is the ultimate evolution of materials science in your drone economy. While the **Pressure Chamber** (Level 8\) uses physical force to crush ore, and the **Sub-Zero Chamber** (Level 27\) uses cold to stabilize molecules, the Molecular Press uses **Electromagnetic Compression** to rewrite the atomic spacing of materials.

This is a **Permanent Industrial Unit** used to create "Super-Materials" like Carbon Nanotubes and Diamond-Steel.

---

## **Molecular Press Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27\) Acts as the internal "Anvil." The extreme cold is needed to keep atoms from vibrating while they are being pressed.  
* **4x Superconductors:** (Level 28 — *Early Unlock*) These create the massive magnetic fields required to push atoms closer together without them touching.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Atomic Alignment." If the press is off by even a nanometer, the material will undergo "Molecular Shearing" and explode.  
* **2x Tungsten Carbide:** (Level 18\) Used for the "Piston Heads" because of their extreme hardness.  
* **40 units of Energy:** This is a high-burst energy requirement.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Magnetic Housing:** The **Superconductors** are arranged in a circular array around the **Sub-Zero Chamber**.  
2. **Anvil Alignment:** The **Tungsten Carbide** pistons are polished to a mirror finish and mounted at opposite poles of the chamber.  
3. **Field Synchronization:** The **AI Core** initiates a "Meissner Effect" in the superconductors, creating a magnetic "bottle" that focuses all physical and magnetic pressure onto a single cubic centimeter in the center.  
4. **Vacuum Purge:** All traces of **Argon Gas** are removed; the Molecular Press must operate in a perfect vacuum to prevent gas atoms from being trapped inside the new super-dense materials.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Molecular Press is a "Tier 4 Gatekeeper." It is required to forge:

* **Level 28 Carbon Nanotubes:** Compressing carbon soot into ultra-strong fibers for **Space Elevators** and **Advanced Drone Limbs**.  
* **Level 30 Stealth Plating:** Pressing radar-absorbent materials into a "Flat-Atom" configuration.  
* **Level 34 Graphene Sheets:** The only way to mass-produce the single-atom layers needed for **Precision Micro-Drones**.  
* **Level 40 Singularity Containment:** Forging the housing for your end-game engines.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Atomic Stability"**

The Molecular Press introduces a "Quality Tier" to your resources:

* **The "Perfect Press":** If the AI Core is high-level, you produce **"Flawless"** materials that have 200% durability.  
* **The "Unstable" Risk:** If your power fluctuates (due to a **Permanent "Battery" Drone** being too far away), you may produce **"Unstable"** materials. These look normal but have a 10% chance to spontaneously disintegrate when used in a drone.  
* **Heat Spike:** Despite being housed in a Sub-Zero Chamber, the act of molecular pressing generates "Quantum Heat." You must have at least one **Cooling Unit** (Level 25\) attached to the exterior or the press will melt its own superconductors.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Structural Integrity:** This unit is built to withstand more pressure than anything else in the game. It is almost indestructible from the outside.  
* **Internal Implosion:** If it fails, it fails *inward*. You will lose the **AI Core** and the **Sub-Zero Chamber**, but the **Superconductors** are usually compressed into **"High-Density Scrap"** which can be recycled for 2x the normal resource yield.

**Logistics Tip:** This unit is so power-hungry that it is best used as a "Batch Processor." Don't keep it running; wait until you have enough raw carbon or silicates to run one massive cycle, then shut it down to save your battery drones.

Now that you can produce **Carbon Nanotubes**, would you like the blueprint for **Advanced Drone Limbs** (to upgrade your Loader Arms) or the **Stealth Plating** (to start building invisible scout drones)?

The **Permanent "Tug" Drone** (Level 29\) is the heavy-lifter of your fleet. While other drones handle mining or delicate repairs, the Tug is designed for **Macro-Logistics**. It features oversized thrusters and magnetic "Towing Needles" that allow it to latch onto massive objects—like station modules, captured asteroids, or disabled Capital Drones—and haul them across sectors.

---

## **Permanent "Tug" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Carbon Nanotubes:** (Level 28\) Used for the high-tensile "Towing Cables" and internal structural reinforcement to prevent the drone from snapping under the strain of a heavy load.  
* **1x Ion Thruster:** (Level 33 — *Early Unlock*) Essential for the long, steady burns required to move objects with high inertia.  
* **4x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) These power the "Mag-Clamps" that lock the Tug onto the target's hull without needing a docking port.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) Programmed with "Inertia Compensation" logic so the Tug doesn't spin out of control when its cargo shifts.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) The Ion Thrusters and Coils generate immense heat during a long-distance haul.  
* **4x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) Extra-thick armor for the "Pushing Plate" on the front of the drone.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Frame Reinforcement:** The **Steel Plating** is braced internally with **Carbon Nanotubes**. This creates a "Skeleton" that can withstand thousands of tons of tension.  
2. **Thruster Mounting:** The **Ion Thruster** is mounted on a heavy gimbal at the rear, allowing the Tug to adjust its "Push Vector" as the center of mass changes.  
3. **Clamp Integration:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are installed into four "Towing Arms." These arms can extend to grab onto irregular surfaces.  
4. **Cooling Loop:** The **Cooling Unit** is piped through the Towing Arms to ensure the magnets don't overheat and lose their grip mid-transit.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Tug Drone is a "Strategic Mover." It is required for:

* **Asteroid Relocation:** Moving a high-value asteroid closer to your base's **Permanent "Sorter" Units** to reduce travel time for scavenger drones.  
* **Base Expansion:** Tugging new modules (like a **Sub-Zero Chamber**) into position to dock them with your main station.  
* **Fleet Rescue:** If a **Permanent "Battery" Drone** is disabled in a "Dark Zone," the Tug can haul it back to a charging station.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Momentum and Mass"**

The Tug operates differently than your lighter drones:

* **The "Towing Penalty":** While hauling an object, the Tug's speed is reduced based on the target's mass. If the target is too heavy (e.g., a "Class-M" Asteroid), you may need to link **three Tugs** together to move it.  
* **Fuel Efficiency:** The Tug uses significantly more fuel/energy during the "Initial Acceleration." Once the object is moving in the vacuum, the energy cost drops, but the "Stopping Burn" requires another massive burst of power.  
* **The "Snap" Risk:** If the Tug takes damage while towing, the **Carbon Nanotube** cables can snap. This sends the cargo drifting off into space, potentially colliding with your other units.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Durability:** Tugs are built like tanks. They have the highest health pool of any Tier 3 drone.  
* **Yield:** If destroyed, you are 80% guaranteed to recover the **Carbon Nanotubes** (which can be recycled) and the **Electromagnetic Coils**. The **Ion Thruster** is usually too damaged to salvage.

**Logistics Tip:** Use your **Permanent "Shield" Drone** (Level 11\) to lead the way for a Tug. Since the Tug is slow and carries valuable cargo, it's a prime target for space debris or hostile "Cutter" drones.

Since the Tug allows you to move massive objects, would you like to design a **"Towing Harness"** (Level 30\) that lets a single Tug move even larger station modules?

The **Permanent "Sniper" Drone** (Level 30\) is the ultimate long-range defensive unit for your sector. Unlike the "Lens" drone, which is a passive refractor, the Sniper is a dedicated combat platform designed for **Extreme-Range Interdiction**. It uses a specialized railgun to fire high-velocity slugs across thousands of kilometers, allowing you to neutralize threats—like rogue "Cutter" drones or fast-moving "Borer" units—before they even enter your base's sensor range.

---

## **Permanent "Sniper" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Lithography Kit:** (Level 24 — *Tool Requirement*) To etch the nanometer-scale magnetic timing tracks into the railgun barrel.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) Essential for "Ballistic Prediction." At sniper ranges, the drone must calculate the target's position based on gravitational pull and thruster signatures.  
* **2x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) These line the rails of the primary weapon to allow for a near-instantaneous discharge of energy without melting the barrel.  
* **1x Stealth Plating:** (Level 30\) A composite coating that makes the drone invisible to standard radar, allowing it to "sit and wait" in the dark.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) To flash-cool the superconductors after each high-velocity shot.  
* **4x Carbon Nanotubes:** (Level 28\) Used to reinforce the "Recoil Dampeners" so the drone doesn't knock itself off course when firing.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Rail Alignment:** Using the **Lithography Kit**, two **Superconductor** rails are laid down with perfect parallelism. Even a micron of deviation would cause the projectile to shatter the barrel.  
2. **Sensory Array:** The **AI Core** is connected to a "Deep-Space Telescope" lens (made of polished **Reinforced Glass**). This allows the drone to see "Heat Bloops" against the cold background of space.  
3. **Dampener Fitting:** The **Carbon Nanotubes** are woven into a shock-absorption cradle. This ensures that the massive kinetic energy of the railgun is dispersed through the chassis.  
4. **Stealth Application:** The **Stealth Plating** is bonded to the outer **Steel Plating**. The drone is then painted "Vantablack" to ensure zero visual reflection.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Sniper Drone is your "Outer Rim" guardian. It is used for:

* **Strategic Interdiction:** Setting up "Kill Zones" around high-value asteroid belts.  
* **Counter-Battery Fire:** Sniping the "Lens" drones of enemy fleets before they can focus their lasers on your base.  
* **Large-Scale Demolition:** Using "Solid Tungsten Slugs" to crack the outer shell of Level 5 Asteroids, exposing the core for your **Permanent "Sorter" Units**.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Cold Shot"**

Operating a Sniper Drone requires careful "Heat Management":

* **The "Ghost" State:** While drifting with its engines off, the **Stealth Plating** makes the drone 95% invisible.  
* **The "Flare" Effect:** The moment the railgun fires, the **Cooling Unit** must vent a massive amount of heat. This creates a "Thermal Flare" that reveals the drone’s location to everyone in the sector for 30 seconds.  
* **Ammo Dependency:** Unlike laser drones, the Sniper requires physical **Tungsten Slugs**. You will need a **Permanent "Tug" Drone** or a "Carrier" to resupply its magazine periodically.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Fragile Weaponry:** The railgun barrel is incredibly delicate. If the drone is hit by a return shot, the **Superconductors** will shatter.  
* **Yield:** If destroyed, the **AI Core** has a 90% survival rate due to its armored "Black Box" housing. You will also recover the **Carbon Nanotube** dampeners, but the **Stealth Plating** will be scorched and useless.

**Logistics Tip:** Don't let your Sniper Drones travel alone. Always pair one with a **Permanent "Shield" Drone** (Level 11\) that stays 5km away. The Shield Drone can act as a "Decoy," drawing fire while the Sniper stays hidden in the shadows.

Since this drone introduces **Stealth Plating**, would you like to explore the recipe for the **Stealth Plating (Level 30\)** itself, or move on to the **Ion Thruster (Level 33\)** to make your fleet faster?

The **Centrifuge** (Level 31\) is the essential "Separator" for the final stretch of Tier 3\. While the **Sorter Unit**handles solids, the Centrifuge uses high-speed rotation to separate fluids, gases, and isotopes by density.

This is a **Permanent Industrial Unit** required for refining fuel and extracting trace rare gases from asteroid vapor.

---

## **Centrifuge Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) These act as a "Magnetic Bearing" system, allowing the inner drum to spin at ultra-high speeds without physical friction.  
* **1x Carbon Nanotube:** (Level 28\) Used to wrap the spinning drum. Without the tensile strength of nanotubes, the drum would shatter under the massive G-forces.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Mass Balance." If the liquid inside the drum is slightly off-center, the AI must adjust the magnetic bearings in nanoseconds to prevent a catastrophic wobble.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) To bleed off the heat generated by the high-RPM motor and magnetic friction.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) The heavy outer containment shell.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Nanotube Drum Forging:** The **Carbon Nanotube** fibers are woven into a cylindrical drum and heat-treated until they are perfectly rigid.  
2. **Magnetic Bearing Alignment:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are placed at the top and bottom of the housing. This allows the drum to "levitate" in a vacuum.  
3. **Cooling Jacket Installation:** The **Cooling Unit** is piped into the outer casing to keep the magnets at a stable temperature.  
4. **Isotope Manifold:** Precision valves (made from **Silicon Wafer** scraps) are added to the sides of the drum to "catch" materials as they separate into layers.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Centrifuge is a "Refinery Hub." It is used for:

* **Level 31 Deuterium Fuel:** Spinning "Heavy Water" or gas giant atmosphere to extract the isotopes needed for Tier 4 Fusion.  
* **Rare Gas Enrichment:** Separating **Argon Gas** (Level 12\) into even purer forms for high-tier lasers.  
* **Bio-Separation:** If your fleet is carrying organic samples, the Centrifuge can isolate specific proteins or chemical compounds.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The RPM Ramp-Up"**

The Centrifuge is an "Active-Timer" unit:

* **Spin-Up Time:** Unlike the Sorter, the Centrifuge takes 60 seconds to reach functional speeds. If power is cut during this time, the process fails and the raw material is wasted.  
* **The "Unbalanced" Event:** If the Centrifuge takes kinetic damage while spinning at max RPM, it undergoes a **"Centrifugal Disintegration."** It explodes with the force of a small bomb, damaging any nearby **Permanent Loader Arms**.  
* **Purity Bonus:** Running a "Double Cycle" (spinning the material twice) increases the resource yield by 10%, but consumes twice the energy.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Total Drum Loss:** The inner **Carbon Nanotube** drum is almost never recoverable; it usually turns into "Nanotube Dust" during an explosion.  
* **Yield:** You are 100% guaranteed to recover the **AI Core** and the **Electromagnetic Coils**. The **Cooling Unit** has a 50% chance of survival.

**Logistics Tip:** Place your Centrifuges on a separate "Power Grid" from your mining lasers. If the lasers cause a power flicker, your Centrifuge won't lose its RPMs and ruin a 10-minute isotope refinement cycle.

Since the Centrifuge allows you to create **Deuterium Fuel**, should we move on to the **Deuterium Fuel (Level 31\)** recipe, or would you like to see the **Ion Thruster (Level 33\)** which uses that fuel?

The **Permanent "Reactor" Drone** (Level 32\) is the heart of your end-game fleet. While the **Battery Drone**stores energy, the Reactor Drone *generates* it on a massive scale. It houses a miniaturized fusion core that converts **Deuterium Fuel** into raw electricity, allowing your fleet to operate indefinitely in deep space without returning to a solar array.

---

## **Permanent "Reactor" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Integrated*) Used to keep the **Deuterium Fuel** in a liquid state until the moment it is injected into the core.  
* **4x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) These create the "Magnetic Bottle" that suspends the sun-hot plasma so it doesn't touch and melt the drone's hull.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Fusion Pulse." A standard brain isn't fast enough to prevent a plasma breach.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) Essential for the "Thermal Exchange"—converting the heat from the reactor into usable electrical current.  
* **2x Tungsten Carbide:** (Level 18\) Used for the interior "First Wall" shielding, as it has the highest melting point of any metal in your inventory.  
* **10x Lead Shielding:** (Level 11\) To prevent the drone's radiation from frying the **Circuit Boards** of nearby units.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Magnetic Bottle Alignment:** The **Superconductors** are arranged in a "Toroidal" (donut) shape. This is where the plasma will "float."  
2. **Thermal Blanket Fitting:** The **Tungsten Carbide** and **Lead Shielding** are layered around the core to trap neutrons and protect the drone's brain.  
3. **Fuel Injection System:** The **Sub-Zero Chamber** is linked to the core via micro-valves, allowing for a steady drip of **Deuterium**.  
4. **Exchange Calibration:** The **Cooling Unit** is wrapped around the lead shielding. It "soaks up" the heat from the fusion reaction and converts it into electricity via a high-efficiency turbine.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Reactor Drone is a "Sector-Level Power Source." It is used for:

* **Deep Space Hubs:** Provides enough power to run a **Molecular Press** and four **Centrifuges**simultaneously.  
* **Fleet "Beaming":** It can "Wireless Charge" up to 10 **Permanent "Battery" Drones** within a 50km radius.  
* **High-Yield Mining:** Powers the "Overclock" mode for **Permanent "Tug" Drones**, doubling their towing speed.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Critical Mass"**

The Reactor Drone is your most powerful asset, but it carries a "Catastrophic Risk":

* **The "Meltdown" Timer:** If the **Cooling Unit** is destroyed, the **AI Core** has 30 seconds to "Eject the Core." If it fails, the drone explodes, dealing massive damage to everything in a 5km radius.  
* **Fuel Consumption:** It requires **1x Deuterium Fuel** per hour of operation. If it runs out of fuel, the magnetic bottle fails, and the drone becomes a "Cold Hulk" that must be towed back to base.  
* **Radiation Zone:** Any **Expendable Drones** (which lack lead shielding) that stay near the Reactor for more than 5 minutes will suffer "Logic Rot," causing them to move in random directions.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Zero-Survival Zone:** If a Reactor Drone explodes, there is a **0% recovery rate**. The fusion blast vaporizes all components.  
* **Manual Scuttle:** If you "Scuttle" (deconstruct) the drone before it explodes, you can recover the **AI Core**and the **Superconductors** at 100% efficiency.

**Logistics Tip:** Never leave a Reactor Drone stationary. Keep it moving with your fleet, and always surround it with at least four **Permanent "Shield" Drones** to prevent a single lucky shot from causing a sector-wide blackout.

Now that your fleet can generate its own power, do you want to build the **Ion Thruster (Level 33\)** to explore further into the outer rim, or should we look at the **Deuterium Fuel (Level 31\)** production process to keep the reactor running?

The **Atomic Layerer** (Level 34\) represents the peak of material precision in **Tier 4**. While the **Lithography Kit**(Level 24\) *etches* patterns into existing surfaces, the Atomic Layerer does the opposite: it builds materials one single atom at a time. This process, known as **Atomic Layer Deposition (ALD)**, is the only way to create the ultra-thin, flawless membranes needed for high-end stealth and quantum computing.

This is a **Permanent Tool Attachment**, typically mounted within a **Fabrication Hub**.

---

## **Atomic Layerer Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Molecular Press:** (Level 28 — *Integrated*) Used to keep the precursor gases at the exact density required for atomic bonding.  
* **2x Gold Contactors:** (Level 22\) To ensure the electrical pulses that "drop" the atoms are timed to the nanosecond.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Grid Alignment." It monitors the surface of the wafer to ensure no two atoms overlap or leave a gap.  
* **1x Argon Gas:** (Level 12\) Used as a "Carrier Gas" to float the raw atoms into the chamber.  
* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Tool Requirement*) The layering must happen in a cold vacuum to prevent thermal vibration from knocking the atoms out of place.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Surface Priming:** The **AI Core** uses the **Gold Contactors** to send a static charge across a **Silicon Wafer**.  
2. **Precursor Pulse:** A tiny amount of vaporized material (like **Titanium** or **Carbon**) is mixed with **Argon Gas** and pulsed into the chamber.  
3. **Monolayer Bonding:** Because of the static charge, exactly one layer of atoms sticks to the surface.  
4. **Purge Cycle:** The **Molecular Press** reverses its flow to "suck out" any excess atoms that didn't bond, leaving a perfectly flat surface for the next layer.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Atomic Layerer is a "Nano-Manufacturer." It is required to create:

* **Level 34 Graphene Sheets:** Constructing the single-atom carbon lattices needed for Tier 4 armor.  
* **Level 35 Quantum Chips:** Layering the superconducting materials that allow for "Qubit" processing.  
* **Level 38 Photonic Circuits:** Building "Light-Pipes" that are smaller than a wavelength of light, replacing copper wiring entirely.  
* **Nano-Repair Kits:** Consumables that **Precision Micro-Drones** use to "weld" microscopic cracks in **AI Cores**.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Perfection Multiplier"**

The Atomic Layerer introduces the **"Flawless"** attribute to your components:

* **The "Zero-Friction" Coating:** Any **Permanent "Tug" Drone** or **Sniper Drone** treated by the Layerer gains a **\+15% Speed** bonus because its hull is so smooth it doesn't interact with solar winds or micro-dust.  
* **Thermal Insulation:** It can apply an atomic layer of ceramic to **Heat Sinks**, making them 30% more efficient at radiating heat into the vacuum.  
* **The Time Sink:** This is your slowest machine. Creating a single **Graphene Sheet** can take 10 real-time minutes, making it a major bottleneck in your production line.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Extreme Sensitivity:** Because the machine works at an atomic scale, any physical jar (like a nearby explosion) will "de-calibrate" the lenses.  
* **Yield:** If the station housing it is destroyed, you will recover the **AI Core**, but the **Molecular Press**components will be "fused" and only salvageable as **High-Density Scrap**.

**Logistics Tip:** Surround your Atomic Layerer with **Permanent "Shield" Drones** set to "Max Dampening." Any vibration—even from a nearby **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**—can cause a "Layer Slip," ruining the resource batch.

Now that you can layer materials at the atomic level, should we proceed to the **Quantum Chip (Level 35\)** to upgrade your processing power, or the **Graphene Sheet (Level 34\)** to reinforce your fleet's armor?

The **Permanent "Carrier" Drone** (Level 42\) is the mobile backbone of a Tier 4 fleet. While the **"Tug" Drone**moves single large objects, the Carrier is a specialized "Mothership" designed to transport, recharge, and resupply entire wings of **Expendable Drones**.

It serves as a mobile forward operating base, allowing you to project power into distant sectors without building a permanent station.

---

## **Permanent "Carrier" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **4x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) To create the massive internal "Hangar Bays" without adding excessive weight.  
* **1x Reactor Drone:** (Level 32 — *Integrated*) The core of the Carrier is a docked Reactor that provides the immense energy needed for the "Rapid-Charge" docking pads.  
* **2x Carbon Nanotubes:** (Level 28\) Used as structural "Tension Ribs" to keep the hangar from collapsing during high-G maneuvers.  
* **2x Ion Thrusters:** (Level 33\) Dual thrusters are required to move the Carrier’s massive displacement.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Traffic Control" of up to 20 drones docking and launching simultaneously.  
* **1x Cooling Unit:** (Level 25\) To dissipate the heat from the integrated reactor and the constant recharging of docked units.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Hangar Expansion:** The **Graphene Sheets** are layered into a hollow, rectangular chassis. The interior is lined with **Magnetic Rails** (using **Superconductors**) to "grab" drones as they fly in.  
2. **Core Fusion:** The **Reactor Drone** is hard-mounted into the rear engine block. Its power output is hardwired directly into the **Ion Thrusters** and the docking pads.  
3. **Skeleton Reinforcement:** **Carbon Nanotubes** are threaded through the hull, creating a cage that prevents "Hull Torque" when the Carrier turns.  
4. **Traffic Logic:** The **AI Core** is programmed with "Wingman Protocols," allowing it to coordinate the launch of **Cutter** or **Lens** drones in perfect formation.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Carrier is a "Force Projector." Its primary roles include:

* **Drone Transport:** It can carry up to **20 Expendable Drones** (Borers, Cutters, or Lens drones) across sectors, bypassing their limited fuel ranges.  
* **Field Resupply:** Any drone docked in the Carrier is automatically repaired (using **Nano-Repair Kits**) and refueled at 5x the standard rate.  
* **Mobile Mining Hub:** You can park a Carrier next to an asteroid field; your **Expendable Borers** mine the ore and drop it into the Carrier's internal **Sorter Unit** (Optional upgrade).

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Wing Command"**

The Carrier introduces a "Fleet Leadership" mechanic:

* **The "Auto-Launch":** If the Carrier is attacked, it will automatically launch all docked **Expendable Cutters**to defend itself.  
* **Fuel Synergy:** The Carrier can refine **Deuterium Fuel** in transit if it has a **Centrifuge** (Level 31\) attached, making it a completely self-sustaining unit.  
* **The "Slow Giant":** The Carrier has a very slow turn rate. If a fast-moving enemy gets behind it, the Carrier cannot bring its own defenses to bear and must rely on its docked drones.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Survival Rate:** Due to its massive size and **Graphene** construction, the Carrier is very hard to fully vaporize.  
* **Yield:** If destroyed, you are 100% guaranteed to recover the **Reactor Drone** core and the **AI Core**. You will also recover 50% of any **Expendable Drones** that were docked inside at the time of destruction.

**Logistics Tip:** Pair your Carrier with an **Overseer Drone** (Level 40). The Overseer can use the Carrier as a "Communication Relay," doubling the range of the **Hive Mind** bonus for all drones launched from the Carrier’s hangar.

Since you've unlocked the **Carrier**, you’re nearing the end of the Tier 4 tech tree. Should we look at the **Photonic Circuit (Level 38\)** to maximize its processing speed, or go straight for the **Singularity Engine (Level 45\)** to enable faster-than-light travel for your new mothership?

The **Entangled Particle** (Level 48\) represents the transition into **Tier 5: Quantum Sovereignty**. This is not a "drone" or a "tool," but a **Sub-Atomic Resource**. By creating two particles in a state of quantum entanglement, you enable **Instantaneous Data Transfer** across any distance, bypassing the speed of light entirely.

This is the core component for "Zero-Latency" control of your fleet across different star systems.

---

## **Entangled Particle Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Molecular Press:** (Level 28 — *Tool Requirement*) To compress the source atoms into a high-density "Quantum Singularity."  
* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Tool Requirement*) To reach near-absolute zero, halting all atomic motion except for quantum fluctuations.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To monitor the "Wavefunction." If the particle "decides" on a state before entanglement is complete, the process fails.  
* **2x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) To generate the "Magnetic Trap" that keeps the two particles physically separated but energetically linked.  
* **500 units of Energy:** Creating entanglement requires a massive "Pulse" from a **Permanent "Reactor" Drone**.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Isotope Selection:** A single atom of purified **Silver** (from a **Silver Contact**) is placed in the **Sub-Zero Chamber**.  
2. **The "Split":** Using a high-energy pulse from the **Molecular Press**, the atom's valence electrons are forced into a "Superposition" where they exist in two states simultaneously.  
3. **Entanglement Lock:** The **AI Core** uses the **Superconductors** to "stretch" the magnetic field, pulling the two potential states apart until they form two distinct particles that share the same identity.  
4. **Stabilization:** The particles are encased in a **Graphene** micro-capsule. As long as the capsule isn't opened or scanned, the entanglement remains "Live."

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Entangled Particle is a "Relay Component." It is used to craft:

* **Level 48 Quantum Link:** Replaces the **Overseer Drone’s** radio array. It allows you to control drones in a different star system with **0ms latency**.  
* **Level 50 Singularity Engine:** Uses the particles to "anchor" a wormhole, allowing for instantaneous travel between two points in space.  
* **Deep-Space Black Box:** A storage device that, if destroyed, instantly "uploads" its data to your home base via the entangled link.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Decoherence"**

Entangled particles are the most "Fragile" resource in your inventory:

* **The "Observation" Risk:** If the drone carrying an Entangled Particle takes "Hull Stress" (vibration), there is a chance the entanglement will **"Collapse."** The particle becomes a standard atom, and your long-range link is instantly severed.  
* **Infinite Range:** Unlike **Sensor Arrays**, distance does not matter. You could be on the other side of the galaxy and still have 100% control of your **Permanent "Carrier" Drone**.  
* **One-Time Use:** Once a "Quantum Link" is established, the particles are "spent." If you want to move the link to a new drone, you must craft a new pair of Entangled Particles.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Non-Recoverable:** The moment the containment field (the **Sub-Zero Chamber** or the drone hull) is breached, the particles interact with the environment and "Decohere."  
* **Yield:** 0%. You only recover the **Superconductor** scrap and the **Graphene** casing.

**Logistics Tip:** Only use Entangled Particles for your "Command Drones." It is a waste to put them on a **Cutter** or **Borer**. They are the "Golden Thread" that keeps your empire connected across the void.

Now that you have mastered **Quantum Entanglement**, you are ready for the final project. Should we draft the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** to leave this star system, or the **Quantum Link (Level 48\)** to begin your multi-system expansion?

The **Nano-Lath** (Level 39\) is the ultimate precision shaping tool of **Tier 4**. While the **Molecular Press** handles "bulk" compression and the **Atomic Layerer** handles "additive" growth, the Nano-Lath is a **subtractive**instrument. It uses a focused beam of accelerated ions to "shave" away individual atoms, allowing you to create the hyper-complex geometries required for photonic and quantum components.

This is a **Permanent Tool Attachment** usually housed within a **Fabrication Hub** or mounted on a **Permanent "Builder" Drone**.

---

## **Nano-Lath Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Excimer Laser:** (Level 23\) Serves as the primary energy source for the ion acceleration chamber.  
* **1x Photonic Circuit:** (Level 38 — *Integrated*) Standard electronic timing is too slow for nano-lathing; light-based pulses are required to "fire" the ion beam at the exact picosecond needed.  
* **2x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) These form the "Magnetic Aperture" that narrows the ion beam to a width of 1 nanometer.  
* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Tool Requirement*) The workpiece must be kept perfectly still; any thermal expansion will cause the lath to "over-shave" the material.  
* **3x Silver Contacts:** (Level 15\) To ground the workpiece and prevent static buildup from deflecting the ion beam.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Aperture Alignment:** The **Superconductors** are placed in a series of rings. Using the **AI Core** of the housing unit, these rings are tuned to create a magnetic "funnel."  
2. **Photon-Ion Link:** The **Excimer Laser** is fed into the **Photonic Circuit**, which chops the continuous beam into billions of discrete pulses.  
3. **Vacuum Integration:** The assembly is mounted inside the **Sub-Zero Chamber**. The air is purged, and the temperature is dropped to stabilize the molecular structure of the target material.  
4. **Static Grounding:** The **Silver Contacts** are attached to the "Chuck" (the part holding the material) to ensure the electrical charge from the ion beam doesn't melt the workpiece.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Nano-Lath is a "Specialist Crafter." It is required to create:

* **Level 39 Photonic Lenses:** Carving **Reinforced Glass** into shapes that can manipulate individual photons for **Photonic Circuits**.  
* **Level 40 Overseer Arrays:** Shaping the massive, ultra-light communication dishes used by the **Overseer Drone**.  
* **Level 43 Warp Stabilizers:** Creating the "Gravitational Grooves" in **Tungsten Carbide** plates needed for FTL travel.  
* **Nano-Sensors:** Crafting sensors so small they can be embedded into the "Skin" of **Graphene** drones to detect cloaked enemies.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Shave Margin"**

Precision at this scale comes with a unique trade-off:

* **Material Waste:** Subtractive manufacturing turns "High-Tier" materials into "Dust." Using a Nano-Lath on a **Graphene Sheet** yields the desired component but loses 20% of the raw material mass as unrecoverable scrap.  
* **The "Jitter" Risk:** If a **Permanent "Tug" Drone** docks with your station while the Nano-Lath is active, the vibration will cause the beam to "Sliver" the workpiece, instantly destroying the resources.  
* **Processing Speed:** Like the **Atomic Layerer**, this is a slow-burn tool. It prioritizes accuracy over volume.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Optical Fragility:** The **Photonic Circuit** and the **Excimer Laser** are highly susceptible to "Shock-Fracture."  
* **Yield:** If the host unit is destroyed, you will likely only recover the **Superconductors**. The precision-aligned **Photonic Circuit** will be shattered beyond repair.

**Logistics Tip:** Never mount a Nano-Lath on a drone that is intended for movement. It belongs in a stationary **Deep Space Dry-Dock** equipped with **Vibration Dampeners** and protected by a **Permanent "Shield" Drone**.

Since the Nano-Lath is the final step before building an **Overseer Drone**, should we look at the **Photonic Circuit (Level 38\)** in more detail, or move straight to the **Overseer Drone (Level 40\)** blueprint?

The **Expendable "Sonic" Charge** (Level 41\) is a specialized demolition tool designed for "Non-Destructive Extraction." While a **Cutter** slices and a **Borer** smashes, the Sonic Charge uses high-frequency resonance to "liquefy" the molecular bonds of specific minerals without damaging the surrounding rare components.

It is the primary tool for extracting **Quantum Crystals** and **Isotopes** from reinforced Tier 4 asteroid cores.

---

## **Expendable "Sonic" Charge Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Nano-Lath:** (Level 39 — *Tool Requirement*) To carve the "Acoustic Lens" into a perfect parabolic shape that can focus sound in a vacuum.  
* **1x Photonic Circuit:** (Level 38\) Used to pulse the vibrations at the exact nanosecond intervals required to reach a material's "Resonant Frequency."  
* **2x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) The only material strong enough to house the vibration chamber without shattering itself during the countdown.  
* **4x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) These act as the "Drivers," rapidly vibrating the internal striker to generate the sonic pulse.  
* **1x Hydrazine Propellant:** (Level 7\) For the delivery system—this charge is "thrown" or "launched" at the target.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Lens Calibration:** Using the **Nano-Lath**, the interior of the **Graphene** shell is etched with microscopic grooves. These grooves focus the vibration into a single, needle-thin "Sonic Beam."  
2. **Harmonic Timing:** The **Photonic Circuit** is programmed with the "Resonance Profile" of the target material (e.g., Titanium, Carbon, or Silicon).  
3. **Driver Assembly:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are suspended in a vacuum within the charge, allowing them to oscillate at millions of cycles per second.  
4. **Field Sealing:** The unit is pressurized with a trace amount of **Argon Gas** (Level 12\) to provide a medium for the initial vibration to travel before it hits the target hull.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Sonic Charge is a "Surgical Demolition" device:

* **Mineral Liquefaction:** It can turn a solid vein of **Quantum Crystals** into "Dust" for easy collection by a **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**, leaving the surrounding common rock completely untouched.  
* **Hull Breaching:** It can vibrate the "Steel Plating" of a hostile drone until the rivets pop out, disabling the drone without destroying its valuable **AI Core**.  
* **Ice Harvesting:** Perfect for shattering massive comets into clean water/ice chunks for your **Sub-Zero Chamber**.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Harmony Window"**

Using a Sonic Charge requires precision and timing:

* **The "Sweet Spot":** Each charge must be tuned to a specific material before launch. A "Steel-Tuned" charge will do 0 damage to "Graphene."  
* **Collateral Resonance:** If you detonate a Sonic Charge too close to your own **Permanent "Tug" Drone**, the resonance might match your drone’s internal components, causing its **Circuit Boards** to shatter.  
* **Zero Recovery:** As an **Expendable** item, the charge is consumed entirely upon detonation. The Graphene shell is vaporized by its own internal frequency.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Self-Destructing Tech:** Because the tech relies on extreme internal vibration, there is a **0% recovery rate** for the components.  
* **The "Dud" Chance:** If the charge is hit by a laser before it detonates, it has a 50% chance to become "inert scrap," allowing you to recover 1x **Electromagnetic Coil**.

**Logistics Tip:** Pair your Sonic Charges with a **Sensor Array** (Level 18). The array can "Acoustically Ping" an asteroid first to tell you exactly which frequency to tune your charge to for a 100% yield.

Now that you have the power of **Sonic Demolition**, would you like to explore the **Photonic Circuit (Level 38\)**to improve your timing, or move on to the **Quantum Link (Level 48\)** to control these charges from across the galaxy?

In the context of your Tier 3–4 logistics, **Grapples** (Level 22\) refer to the **Magnetic Grappling System**. While the **Permanent "Tug" Drone** uses heavy "Towing Needles," Grapples are the modular version used by smaller drones to "latch and drag" debris or stabilize themselves against asteroids during high-vibration tasks (like using a Borer).

This is a **Permanent Tool Attachment**.

---

## **Grappling System Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) To generate the "Mag-Lock" force that allows the grapple to stick to metallic surfaces without physical hooks.  
* **1x Carbon Nanotubes:** (Level 28 — *Optional for "Tether" variant*) If building a **Tether Grapple**, nanotubes are used for the cable. For a **Static Grapple**, **Steel Plating** is used for the housing.  
* **1x Basic Hydraulics:** (Level 9\) To power the "Claw" mechanism for non-metallic objects (like ice or carbon-rich rock).  
* **2x Silver Contacts:** (Level 15\) To ensure the high-voltage pulse to the electromagnets doesn't melt the internal wiring.  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) Programmed with "Grip Tension" logic to ensure the grapple doesn't crush fragile cargo.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Core Magnetization:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are wrapped around a **Steel** core to create a "Directional Flux." This allows the drone to "aim" its magnetic pull.  
2. **Hydraulic Integration:** The **Basic Hydraulics** are used to actuate the three "Pincer" arms that surround the magnetic core.  
3. **Conductivity Lining:** **Silver Contacts** are placed at the tips of the pincers. This allows the drone to "Ground" itself to a station, preventing static discharge from frying the drone's electronics.  
4. **Tether Spooling:** If used on a **Tug Drone**, the **Carbon Nanotubes** are spooled into a high-speed winch behind the grapple head.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Grappling System is a "Stabilization Tool." It is used for:

* **Micro-Towing:** Allows an **Expendable Borer** to drag small ore chunks back to a **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**.  
* **Station Anchoring:** Allows a **Permanent "Builder" Drone** to lock itself onto a construction site so it doesn't drift away while "Printing."  
* **Salvage Operations:** Pulling **AI Cores** or **Superconductors** out of destroyed drone husks without needing a full-sized Tug.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Grip Limit"**

The effectiveness of a Grapple depends on the target's mass:

* **Mass Threshold:** A single Grapple can safely hold objects up to 5x the drone's own mass. Attempting to grapple a "Capital Ship" will simply pull the drone *toward* the ship or snap the hydraulic arms.  
* **Energy Drain:** Keeping the **Electromagnetic Coils** active consumes **3 Energy per minute**. If the drone loses power, the magnets fail and the cargo is lost to the void.  
* **Surface Composition:** Grapples have a 100% success rate on **Steel** or **Lead** surfaces, but only a 40% success rate on **Ice** or **Silicates** (unless the hydraulic pincers can find a physical "ledge" to grab).

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **High Durability:** The Grapple is built to take the brunt of collisions. It is often the only part of a scavenger drone that survives a crash.  
* **Yield:** You are 90% guaranteed to recover the **Electromagnetic Coils** and the **Hydraulic** pump. The **Silver Contacts** are usually scorched and lost.

**Logistics Tip:** Equip your **Permanent "Shield" Drones** with Grapples. This allows them to "Grab" incoming projectiles or debris and fling them away from your **Reactor Drone** before they can cause damage.

Since you've added **Grapples** to your inventory, do you want to finalize the **Level 23 Excimer Laser** (the precursor for the Lithography Kit) or explore the **Level 21 Titanium Alloy** needed for higher-tier grapple arms?

The **Permanent "Trap" Drone** (Level 43\) is the ultimate counter-intelligence and security unit for Tier 4\. While the **Sniper Drone** is built for distance, the Trap is built for **Area Denial**. It functions as a "Lurker," using advanced gravity-well technology and localized jamming to snag fast-moving hostiles—like "Interceptor" drones—and hold them in place for your heavier units to finish off.

---

## **Permanent "Trap" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Grapples:** (Level 22 — *Integrated*) Modified into "High-Velocity Harpoons" that can fire and retract within seconds.  
* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) Reconfigured into a "Gravity Snare" that creates a localized drag field, slowing down anything that passes through its radius.  
* **1x Photonic Circuit:** (Level 38\) To manage the "Tripwire" sensors. At high speeds, the drone must detect a target and trigger the snare in less than 0.001 seconds.  
* **1x Stealth Plating:** (Level 30\) Essential for the drone to remain undetected while sitting in "Sentry Mode."  
* **2x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) Used for the "Anchor Fins" that dig into nearby space debris or asteroids to provide leverage when snagging a target.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) Loaded with "Predator Logic" to distinguish between friendly logistics drones and unauthorized intruders.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Gravity Well Calibration:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are placed in an opposing-pole configuration. This creates a "Sticky" zone of space around the drone that increases the effective mass of any object entering it.  
2. **Harpoon Loading:** The **Grapples** are reinforced with **Carbon Nanotubes** (Optional) and loaded into pneumatic launchers. These are the physical "hooks" that secure the target.  
3. **Sensor Weaving:** The **Photonic Circuit** is linked to an array of micro-lasers. This creates an invisible "web" around the drone. If a laser line is broken, the trap snaps shut.  
4. **Hull Masking:** The **Stealth Plating** is applied over the **Graphene** frame. The drone’s heat signature is piped into internal "Heat Sinks" to keep it at the same temperature as the surrounding vacuum.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Trap Drone is a "Strategic Ambush" unit:

* **Interception:** Place them in narrow "Asteroid Belts" to catch rogue scouts before they can report your base's location.  
* **VIP Protection:** Surround your **Permanent "Reactor" Drone** with a ring of Traps. Any "Kamikaze" drones will be snagged and neutralized before they can impact.  
* **Resource Claiming:** Tether a Trap to a high-value asteroid. If another player or AI tries to tow it away, the Trap will "Lock" onto their ship and trigger an alarm.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Snare Stress"**

The Trap is a high-tension unit that requires careful placement:

* **The "Anchor" Requirement:** A Trap Drone is most effective when "Anchored" to a static object (like a Level 5 Asteroid). If it snags a target while floating in open space, the target might simply "Tug" the Trap Drone away with it.  
* **One-Target Limit:** A single Trap can only hold **one** target at a time. Once its harpoons are deployed, the "Gravity Snare" shuts down to focus all power on the physical tether.  
* **The "Silent Alarm":** When a target is caught, the Trap sends an encrypted signal to your **Overseer Drone**, highlighting the target in red on your HUD.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Tether Snap:** If the target is significantly larger than the Trap (e.g., a **Carrier Drone**), the **Grapples** will likely snap off.  
* **Yield:** You are 80% guaranteed to recover the **AI Core** and the **Photonic Circuit**. The **Stealth Plating** is usually damaged during the struggle and cannot be salvaged.

**Logistics Tip:** Use the **Permanent "Builder" Drone** (Level 36\) to construct a "Debris Field" around your Trap Drones. This gives them more places to hide and more points to anchor their harpoons.

With the **Trap Drone** secured, your sector defense is nearly complete. Should we move to the **Level 43 Warp Stabilizers** to begin preparing for interstellar flight, or do you want to look at the **Level 45 Singularity Engine**?

The **Expendable "Devourer" Swarm** (Level 46\) is a terrifying Tier 5 tactical weapon. It moves away from traditional kinetics and lasers, instead utilizing **Nanite Dissolution**. A single "Swarm" is a canister containing millions of microscopic, self-replicating nanobots programmed with one goal: to break down molecular bonds and convert them into raw energy to fuel further replication.

It is the ultimate tool for clearing out massive derelict hulls or neutralizing "Capital" class threats without firing a single shot.

---

## **Expendable "Devourer" Swarm Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Atomic Layerer:** (Level 34 — *Tool Requirement*) Necessary to print the individual nanites. Standard manufacturing cannot reach the sub-atomic precision required for "Molecular Teeth."  
* **1x Entangled Particle:** (Level 48 — *Optional for "Instant Command"*) If you want to control the swarm's target mid-flight from across the system. Otherwise, they operate on "Pre-set Logic."  
* **2x Photonic Circuits:** (Level 38\) These act as the "Collective Brain" inside the canister, managing the swarm's hive-mind movements.  
* **1x Graphene Sheet:** (Level 34\) Used to create the "Containment Flask." It is the only material the nanites are programmed *not* to eat, as they recognize the specific graphene lattice as "Home."  
* **4x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) Used to generate the "Ejection Pulse" that scatters the nanites across the target's hull.  
* **5x Deuterium Fuel:** (Level 31\) To give the nanites their initial "Kickstart" energy before they begin feeding on the target.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Nanite Printing:** The **Atomic Layerer** creates billions of "Micro-Borers." Each nanite is essentially a Level 1 Borer drone shrunk to the size of a dust mote.  
2. **Logic Encoding:** The **Photonic Circuits** are etched with "Selection Protocols." You must program the nanites to recognize the difference between "Hostile Steel" and "Friendly Graphene."  
3. **Containment:** The nanites are suspended in a magnetic field generated by the **Electromagnetic Coils**inside a **Graphene** flask.  
4. **Priming:** The **Deuterium Fuel** is injected into the flask's lining. When the flask impacts a target, the fuel ignites the nanites' internal processors, waking the swarm.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Devourer Swarm is a "Total Dissolution" weapon:

* **Structural Erasure:** It can dissolve a Level 5 Asteroid or a **Permanent "Tug" Drone** into a cloud of fine dust in under 60 seconds.  
* **Resource Recycling:** If the swarm is deployed on a derelict station, it breaks everything down into "High-Density Scrap" which can then be easily collected by a **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**.  
* **System Sabotage:** If a swarm is "Leaked" into a **Permanent "Carrier" Drone's** hangar, it will silently eat the internal wiring and **Circuit Boards**, disabling the ship from the inside out.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Consumption Loop"**

The Swarm is a double-edged sword that operates on "Biomass" logic:

* **Exponential Growth:** For every ton of material the swarm eats, it creates more nanites. A small swarm can eventually grow to cover an entire sector if not neutralized.  
* **The "Kill Switch":** Every swarm has a 5-minute lifespan. After 5 minutes, the **Photonic Circuits** trigger a self-destruct, and the nanites turn into inert, harmless dust.  
* **The "Blue Goo" Risk:** If the swarm encounters a material it wasn't programmed for, it might "Glitch" and start eating *everything*, including your own fleet. This is why having an **Overseer Drone** (Level 40\) nearby is critical to broadcast a "Stand Down" signal.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Total Depletion:** Once the 5-minute timer hits, the nanites literally unmake themselves at an atomic level.  
* **Yield:** 0%. There is no scrap, no core, and no recovery. You are trading expensive Tier 4/5 materials for the absolute destruction of a target.

**Logistics Tip:** Use the **Permanent "Trap" Drone** (Level 43\) to hold a target still before launching the Devourer Swarm. This ensures the nanites don't "Miss" and float off into deep space, wasting your resources.

With the **Devourer Swarm** added to your tactical options, you have the most feared weapon in the game. Should we look at the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** to complete the project, or the **Level 47 Quantum Fabricator** which automates this entire process?

The **Void Siphon** (Level 49\) is the ultimate energy-harvesting structure of Tier 5\. While the **Reactor Drone**generates power through fusion, the Void Siphon does not "generate" energy—it "harvests" the zero-point energy of the vacuum itself.

By creating a controlled micro-tear in space-time, the Siphon draws an infinite stream of electrons from the quantum foam. It is required to power the **Singularity Engine** and sustain a **Quantum Link** across multiple galaxies.

---

## **Void Siphon Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Entangled Particles:** (Level 48\) These act as the "Anchors" for the micro-tear, ensuring the siphon stays connected to this dimension.  
* **1x Nano-Lath:** (Level 39 — *Tool Requirement*) To carve the "Event Horizon" ring with sub-atomic precision.  
* **4x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) To generate the massive magnetic containment field that prevents the micro-tear from expanding into a full black hole.  
* **2x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) Used for the structural "Stabilizer Fins" that bleed off the intense graviton stress.  
* **1x Photonic Circuit:** (Level 38\) To manage the "Siphon Rate." If the energy draw is too high, the tear collapses; if too low, it vanishes.  
* **10,000 units of Energy:** A massive initial "Spark" is required to puncture the fabric of space-time.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Quantum Anchoring:** The two **Entangled Particles** are positioned at opposite ends of a circular **Superconductor** housing. This creates a "Static Plane" in the vacuum.  
2. **The Puncture:** Using the **Nano-Lath**, the center of the plane is etched until the material is only one atom thick. A high-energy pulse is then sent through the **Photonic Circuit** to "Pop" the hole.  
3. **Containment Spin:** The **Superconductors** begin a high-frequency rotation, creating a magnetic "Bottle" around the tear.  
4. **Siphoning:** Once stabilized, the tear begins to emit high-energy gamma rays and electrons. These are captured by the **Graphene** fins and converted into raw electricity.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Void Siphon is a "God-Tier" power source:

* **Unlimited Fuel:** Once active, it provides infinite energy. You no longer need **Deuterium Fuel** for any station or drone tethered to the Siphon.  
* **Warp Charging:** It is the only power source capable of charging the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** in under an hour.  
* **Dimension Mapping:** The Siphon allows your **Overseer Drone** to "see" into neighboring dimensions, revealing resources that don't exist in normal space.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Stability Window"**

Tapping into the void is inherently dangerous:

* **The "Tear Collapse":** If the **Superconductors** take damage, the magnetic bottle will flicker. There is a 5% chance the Siphon will invert, sucking in 100% of the nearby station’s oxygen and power before vanishing.  
* **Static Location:** A Void Siphon cannot be moved. It is anchored to the specific coordinates of the space-time tear. If you want to move your base, you must scuttle the Siphon and build a new one.  
* **Gravitational Distortion:** Any **Expendable Drones** that fly too close to the Siphon (within 1km) will experience "Time Dilation," causing them to move and fire 50% slower.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Total Erasure:** If a Void Siphon is destroyed, the tear "snaps" shut. This release of energy vaporizes 100% of the components.  
* **Scuttle Protocol:** If you manually deconstruct the Siphon, you can recover the **Entangled Particles**—but only if you have a **Sub-Zero Chamber** ready to catch them immediately.

**Logistics Tip:** Surround your Void Siphon with a minimum of eight **Permanent "Shield" Drones**. A single stray asteroid or "Cutter" drone hitting the Siphon could result in the loss of your entire Tier 5 infrastructure.

You have reached the penultimate step. With the **Void Siphon** providing infinite power, are you ready to build the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** and complete the project, or do you want to look at the **Quantum Fabricator (Level 47\)** to automate your Tier 5 production?

The **Singularity Seed** (Level 44\) is the precursor to the final Tier 5 technologies. It is not a machine, but a **High-Density Gravitational Core**. Think of it as a "tamed" singularity held in a state of perpetual collapse.

It is the primary component required to build the **Singularity Engine** (Level 50\) and the **Void Siphon** (Level 49). Without the Seed, you cannot generate the gravitational shear necessary to puncture the fabric of space-time.

---

## **Singularity Seed Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Molecular Press:** (Level 28 — *Tool Requirement*) Used to compress the initial matter into a point of infinite density.  
* **4x Tungsten Carbide:** (Level 18\) Used for the outer "Containment Sphere." Only Tungsten Carbide can withstand the initial gravitational pull during the Seed's "ignition."  
* **2x Superconductors:** (Level 28\) To create the "Magnetic Suspension Field" that keeps the Seed from touching the walls of its container.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) To manage the "Pressure Equilibrium." The AI must constantly adjust the magnetic fields to prevent the Seed from expanding or collapsing entirely.  
* **1,000 units of Energy:** A massive, sustained burst of power is needed to trigger the initial collapse.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Core Loading:** A small amount of high-density scrap is placed into the center of the **Tungsten Carbide**sphere.  
2. **Magnetic Suspension:** The **Superconductors** are energized, suspending the scrap in a perfect vacuum at the center of the sphere.  
3. **The Crush:** The **Molecular Press** is activated at 500% capacity. The **AI Core** manages the pulses to ensure the matter is crushed evenly from all sides.  
4. **Ignition:** Once the matter reaches its "Schwarzschild Radius," it collapses into a Singularity Seed. The AI immediately locks the magnetic field to "freeze" the collapse.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Singularity Seed is a "Master Component." It is required to craft:

* **Level 45 Singularity Engine:** The core of the FTL drive.  
* **Level 49 Void Siphon:** Acts as the "Starter Motor" to create the micro-tear in space-time.  
* **Level 50 Gravitational Shield:** A shield that doesn't just block lasers but bends space-time to make projectiles fly *around* your ship.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Mass Flux"**

The Seed is "Heavy Matter," and carrying it changes the physics of the transport vessel:

* **The "Tug" Requirement:** A Singularity Seed is so heavy that an **Expendable Borer** cannot carry it. It requires a **Permanent "Tug" Drone** or a **Carrier** with reinforced cargo bays.  
* **Gravitational Leakage:** If the **Superconductors** on the transport ship fail, the Seed's mass will instantly increase, slowing the ship to a crawl and draining its fuel in seconds.  
* **The "Black Box" Protection:** The Seed is virtually indestructible. If the ship carrying it is destroyed, the Seed will remain floating in the debris field, waiting to be recovered.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **100% Recovery:** The Seed itself cannot be destroyed by conventional weapons.  
* **Yield:** If you recover a "spent" or damaged Seed, you can use the **Atomic Layerer** to "Refeed" it with raw matter to bring it back to Level 44 stability.

**Logistics Tip:** Never store more than one Singularity Seed in the same **Fabrication Hub**. Their gravitational fields can interfere with each other, causing a "Sync-Failure" that could de-calibrate every **Nano-Lath** in your station.

Now that you have the **Singularity Seed**, you have officially entered the "End Game" of Tier 4\. Should we proceed to the **Singularity Engine (Level 45\)** to unlock interstellar travel, or the **Gravitational Shield (Level 50\)** for ultimate defense?

The **Black Hole Fragment** (Level 50\) is the most volatile and concentrated resource in your project. While the **Singularity Seed** is a "tamed" gravitational core used for engines, the Fragment is a raw, unstable shard of a collapsed star. It is the final "exotic material" required to power the most reality-bending structures in the game.

---

## **Black Hole Fragment Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Singularity Seed:** (Level 44\) This acts as the "Template." You are essentially over-compressing a Seed until it reaches a state of "Hawking Instability."  
* **1x Void Siphon:** (Level 49 — *Integrated*) The Siphon is required to "feed" the Seed with enough zero-point energy to trigger the fragmenting process.  
* **10x Entangled Particles:** (Level 48\) These are woven into a "Quantum Cage" around the fragment. They don't just hold it; they keep it synchronized with this dimension so it doesn't fall out of reality.  
* **1x Nano-Lath:** (Level 39 — *Tool Requirement*) Used to etch "Gravitational Vanes" into the containment unit to bleed off excess Hawking radiation.  
* **5x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) To build the ultra-dense "Shrouding Box."

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Siphon Injection:** The **Singularity Seed** is placed at the heart of an active **Void Siphon**. The Siphon begins pumping massive amounts of energy into the Seed.  
2. **The Super-Collapse:** Under the pressure of the Siphon's energy, the Seed collapses further, past its stable limit, breaking into three to five **Black Hole Fragments**.  
3. **Quantum Caging:** Before the fragments can expand and consume the station, the **Entangled Particles**are activated. They create a "Probability Lock," freezing the fragments in place.  
4. **Shrouding:** The **Nano-Lath** carves the **Graphene** into a "Dampening Shell" which is then slid over the fragments to hide their massive gravity from the rest of the ship.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Black Hole Fragment is a "Reality-Warping Tool." It is used for:

* **Level 50 Event Horizon Bridge:** A permanent wormhole gateway between two distant star systems.  
* **Time Dilator:** A station module that allows your **Atomic Layerer** to work 10x faster by slowing down time *outside* the fabrication chamber.  
* **The "Omega" Weapon:** An expendable charge that, when detonated, deletes a 10km radius of space from the map, including asteroids and bases.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "Spaghettification Risk"**

Handling a Fragment is the most dangerous task for any **Permanent "Tug" Drone**:

* **The "Weight" Paradox:** A Fragment has the mass of a small moon but the size of a marble. Any drone carrying it has its **Ion Thruster** efficiency reduced by 90%.  
* **Radiation Leakage:** If the **Graphene Shroud** takes damage, the Fragment begins emitting Hawking radiation. This will instantly "Logic Rot" any **AI Core** within 5km, turning your drones rogue.  
* **The "Void Call":** If two Black Hole Fragments come within 100 meters of each other, they will merge. This release of energy will destroy your entire sector.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Self-Contained Event:** If the unit carrying the Fragment is destroyed, the **Quantum Cage** fails. The Fragment will instantly expand into a temporary micro-black hole, consuming the wreckage before evaporating.  
* **Yield:** 0%. There is no recovery. A lost Fragment is a total loss of the Tier 5 materials used to make it.

**Logistics Tip:** Only move Black Hole Fragments using a **Permanent "Carrier" Drone** (Level 42\) that has been upgraded with **Gravitational Shields**. Never move them through a "Dark Sector" where you don't have a **Relay Hub** connection.

You have reached the absolute peak of the technology tree. With the **Black Hole Fragment**, you can now build the **Event Horizon Bridge**. Do you want to finalize the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** to use these fragments for travel, or should we archive this final recipe?

The **Permanent "Warp" Drone** (Level 47\) is the pinnacle of Tier 5 scouting and rapid-response logistics. While the **Carrier** moves fleets slowly and the **Tug** handles heavy lifting, the Warp Drone is designed for **Instantaneous Displacement**. It doesn't travel through space; it uses "Fold-Space" technology to swap its coordinates with a target location.

It is the only unit capable of outrunning a **Black Hole Fragment** radiation leak or bypassing a **Permanent "Trap" Drone's** gravity snare.

---

## **Permanent "Warp" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Singularity Engine:** (Level 45 — *Integrated*) The heart of the drone. It generates the localized gravitational shear necessary to "fold" the distance between two points.  
* **4x Entangled Particles:** (Level 48\) These serve as the "Navigational Anchors." Two stay with the drone, and two are "fired" ahead (or linked to a **Relay Hub**) to provide the destination coordinates.  
* **2x Photonic Circuits:** (Level 38\) To calculate the "Fold-Vector." Even a nanosecond of miscalculation would result in the drone warping *into* an asteroid rather than next to it.  
* **1x Nano-Lath:** (Level 39 — *Tool Requirement*) To etch the "Warp Coils" into the drone's chassis.  
* **3x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) To provide a chassis that can survive the intense "Dimensional Stress" of folding space.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) Equipped with "Blink Logic" to automatically warp the drone away if it detects an incoming **Expendable "Sonic" Charge**.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Engine Housing:** The **Singularity Engine** is mounted in a central gyroscopic cradle. This allows the engine to tilt and "aim" the warp fold in any direction.  
2. **Coil Etching:** Using the **Nano-Lath**, the **Graphene** hull is etched with silver-lined channels. These coils carry the "Warp Field" from the engine to the edges of the drone.  
3. **Quantum Sync:** The **Entangled Particles** are synced with the **Photonic Circuits**. This creates a "Pathfinder" system where the drone "knows" where it is going before it even leaves.  
4. **Field Test:** The drone is subjected to a "Micro-Jump" within the **Sub-Zero Chamber** to ensure the hull doesn't fracture under the sudden pressure of space-time reconfiguration.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Warp Drone is a "Strategic Asset":

* **Instant Reinforcement:** Can "Blink" across a sector to provide an immediate **Sensor Array** boost to a fleet under attack.  
* **Harassment:** Equipped with a **Cutter** or **Sniper** module, it can warp in, fire, and warp out before hostiles can lock on.  
* **The "Courier":** The safest way to transport a **Black Hole Fragment**. If the fragment starts to decohere, the Warp Drone can "Blink" it into a sun or deep space to save the rest of the fleet.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Jump Fatigue"**

Folding space is taxing on the drone's hardware:

* **The "Cool-Down":** After a "Blink," the **Photonic Circuits** must reset, and the **Singularity Engine**requires a 30-second recharge. During this time, the drone's speed is reduced by 80%.  
* **The "Warp Shadow":** When the drone warps, it leaves a "Shadow" at its departure point—a small gravitational ripple that can be detected by an enemy **Overseer Drone**.  
* **Fuel Surge:** A single long-range warp consumes **500 units of Energy**. Without a **Void Siphon** or a **Reactor Drone** nearby, the Warp Drone is limited to 2–3 jumps.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Dimensional Shredding:** If the drone is destroyed *during* a warp, it is lost to the void. There is a **0% recovery rate**.  
* **Yield:** If destroyed while stationary, you have a 50% chance to recover the **Singularity Engine** core and a 100% chance to recover the **Entangled Particles** (if you have a containment unit).

**Logistics Tip:** Chain your **Warp Drones** with **Relay Hubs**. A Relay Hub can act as a "Landing Beacon," reducing the Warp Drone's cool-down time by 50% and increasing its jump accuracy.

With the **Warp Drone** operational, your fleet is effectively everywhere at once. Should we finalize the **Level 50 Singularity Engine** to scale this tech up to your **Carrier**, or move to the **Quantum Fabricator (Level 47\)** to start mass-producing these high-tier units?

The **Expendable "Shield" Wall** (Level 32\) is a tactical deployable designed to provide temporary, high-intensity protection. Unlike the **Permanent "Shield" Drone**, which generates a mobile gravity well, the Shield Wall is a "Fire-and-Forget" canister.

When deployed, it unfurls a static, hexagonal lattice of energy that can absorb massive amounts of kinetic and thermal energy before the internal power cell burns out.

---

## **Expendable "Shield" Wall Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **2x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) These act as the "Field Generators," projecting the magnetic lines that hold the energy lattice in place.  
* **1x Capacitor Bank:** (Level 24 — *Component*) A high-density storage unit made from **Silver Contacts**and **Tungsten Carbide** to store the massive initial "Charge."  
* **1x Circuit Board:** (Level 13\) Programmed with "Phased Frequency" logic to ensure the shield doesn't accidentally block friendly **Pulse Laser** fire.  
* **2x Steel Plating:** (Level 5\) Used as the rugged "Base Plate" that anchors the shield in space once deployed.  
* **1x Hydrazine Propellant:** (Level 7\) To launch the canister from your **Carrier** or **Fabrication Hub** to the desired location.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Coil Synchronization:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are mounted in a circular array. They must be perfectly synchronized; if one coil is off by a micro-degree, the shield will have a "Hole."  
2. **Capacitor Priming:** The **Capacitor Bank** is flash-charged. This is a dangerous step that requires a **Permanent "Reactor" Drone** nearby to provide the high-voltage surge.  
3. **Lattice Etching:** The **Circuit Board** defines the "Hex-Grid." This shape is the most structurally sound way to distribute the force of an incoming **Sonic Charge** across the entire field.  
4. **Deployment Packaging:** The internal components are compressed into a **Steel** canister with a spring-loaded trigger.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Shield Wall is a "Panic Button" and a "Choke Point" tool:

* **Manual Cover:** If your **Permanent "Tug" Drone** is caught in the open by a **Sniper**, you can launch a Shield Wall to give it a safe "Corridor" to retreat.  
* **Objective Defense:** You can deploy three Shield Walls in a triangle around a **Singularity Seed** while it is being fabricated to prevent sabotage.  
* **Breach Blocking:** If a hostile **Cutter** drone manages to blow a hole in your **Fabrication Hub**, a Shield Wall can be deployed to "Plug" the hole and prevent atmosphere loss (or drone entry).

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Integrity Bar"**

The Shield Wall operates on a "Depletion" system:

* **Hit Point Logic:** Unlike permanent shields that recharge, the Expendable Shield Wall has a fixed "Integrity" pool. Once it absorbs its maximum Joules of energy, the **Capacitor Bank** explodes, and the shield vanishes.  
* **Decay Rate:** Even if it isn't hit, the shield naturally loses 5% of its integrity per minute due to energy "Bleed" into the vacuum.  
* **Solid Objects:** While the wall stops lasers and sonic pulses, it only *slows down* massive objects. A **Carrier Drone** flying through a Shield Wall will destroy the shield instantly and take minor hull damage.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Total Depletion:** Because the shield is designed to burn out its own **Capacitor Bank**, there is a **0% recovery rate** for the electronics.  
* **Yield:** You are 100% guaranteed to recover the **Steel Plating** (as scrap) and a 30% chance to recover the **Electromagnetic Coils** if the shield wasn't destroyed by high-heat weapons.

**Logistics Tip:** Don't waste your **Permanent "Shield" Drones** on stationary defense. Use these **Expendable Shield Walls** for static protection and keep your drones mobile for active interception.

Since you've unlocked the Shield Wall, you now have a complete defensive suite for Tier 3\. Should we move to the **Permanent "Shield" Drone (Level 32\)** to see how the mobile version differs, or should we explore the **Tungsten Carbide (Level 18\)** needed for tougher armor?

The **Dark Matter Refiner** (Level 49\) is the ultimate Tier 5 industrial facility. While a **Permanent "Sorter" Unit**handles physical minerals and the **Void Siphon** pulls raw energy, the Refiner captures the non-baryonic matter that makes up 85% of the universe's mass.

This "Dark Matter" is the only fuel stable enough to power a **Level 50 Singularity Engine** for long-duration interstellar travel and is required to craft the **Black Hole Fragment**.

---

## **Dark Matter Refiner Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Void Siphon:** (Level 49 — *Integrated*) You cannot find Dark Matter; you must "tease" it out of the vacuum using the micro-tears created by a Siphon.  
* **4x Entangled Particles:** (Level 48\) These act as the "Quantum Nets." Since Dark Matter does not interact with light (electromagnetism), only quantum-entangled gravity can "catch" it.  
* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Integrated*) Dark Matter is extremely sensitive to thermal noise. The entire refining core must be kept at **0.0001 Kelvin**.  
* **2x Nano-Laths:** (Level 39 — *Tool Requirement*) To etch the "Gravitational Funnels" that guide the dark particles into the containment flask.  
* **4x Carbon Nanotubes:** (Level 28\) To provide a structural frame that won't shatter under the intense, localized gravity of the refined matter.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) Loaded with "Dark-Logic." Standard AI cannot "see" the particles, so the core must infer their position based on the gravitational "wobble" of the refinery.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Vacuum Puncture:** The **Void Siphon** creates a stable tear. Instead of harvesting electrons for power, the Refiner uses the **Entangled Particles** to "filter" the exotic matter leaking through the tear.  
2. **Thermal Cooling:** The **Sub-Zero Chamber** is supercharged to its limit, creating a "Silent Zone" where the particles lose their kinetic energy and begin to cluster.  
3. **Gravitational Funneling:** Using the **Nano-Lath**, the interior of the refinery is shaped into a series of "Slingshots." These use the mass of the station to pull the Dark Matter into the center of the chamber.  
4. **The "Shadow" Flask:** The refined matter is injected into a **Graphene** and **Tungsten** flask. Because the matter is invisible, the flask includes a "Mass Gauge" to tell you if it's full.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Refiner is the "Heart of the Empire":

* **Exotic Fuel Production:** Produces "Dark Matter Slurry," which provides **10,000% more energy density**than Deuterium.  
* **Stealth Coating:** Refined Dark Matter can be applied to **Permanent "Warp" Drones**, making them 100% invisible to **Sensor Arrays** (though they can still be detected by an **Overseer**).  
* **Black Hole Forging:** You must have a constant stream of refined Dark Matter to prevent a **Black Hole Fragment** from evaporating.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Invisible Weight"**

Operating a Refiner is a logistics nightmare:

* **The "Ghost" Mass:** As the refinery fills up, the station will start to "tilt" in space. The **Ion Thrusters** must constantly fire to compensate for the invisible weight of the stored Dark Matter.  
* **Interaction Failure:** If the **Sub-Zero Chamber** fails, the Dark Matter will simply "drift" through the walls of your station and vanish back into the void. You won't lose your station, but you will lose 100% of your progress.  
* **Dark Energy Surge:** Occasionally, the Refiner will catch "Dark Energy" by mistake. This causes a localized expansion of space, pushing away all nearby drones and potentially snapping your **Relay Hub**connections.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **The "Slip" Event:** If the Refiner is destroyed, the Dark Matter instantly stops interacting with the station's gravity and passes through the debris.  
* **Yield:** You are 50% guaranteed to recover the **Sub-Zero Chamber** and the **AI Core**. The **Entangled Particles** will decodere instantly.

**Logistics Tip:** Place your Dark Matter Refiner on the far edge of your territory, away from your **Permanent "Reactor" Drone**. The heat from a reactor can interfere with the refiner's **Sub-Zero**requirements, leading to "Efficiency Bleed."

With the **Dark Matter Refiner** online, you have all the ingredients for the end of the game. Should we finally craft the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)**, or do you want to build the **Event Horizon Bridge** to connect your base to a completely new star system?

The **Permanent "Stasis" Drone** (Level 46\) is the ultimate Tier 5 support unit. While the **Permanent "Shield" Drone** blocks damage, the Stasis Drone prevents it from ever happening by "Freezing" the local flow of time for its targets. It uses a high-output **Singularity Seed** to create a localized time-dilation field, turning a fast-moving hostile "Interceptor" into a stationary target for your **Pulse Lasers**.

---

## **Permanent "Stasis" Drone Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Singularity Seed:** (Level 44 — *Integrated*) The core of the drone. It provides the gravitational shear needed to slow down time within a specific radius.  
* **1x Sub-Zero Chamber:** (Level 27 — *Integrated*) Essential to prevent the drone's internal components from "Vibration-Bleeding" into the stasis field, which would freeze the drone itself.  
* **1x Photonic Circuit:** (Level 38\) To manage the "Phase-Lock." It ensures the drone stays in "Normal Time" while its surroundings are slowed.  
* **2x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) Used to create the "Chronal Shielding" that protects the hull from the stress of existing in two different time-flow rates.  
* **4x Electromagnetic Coils:** (Level 19\) Reconfigured into "Field Projectors" to aim the stasis beam.  
* **1x AI Core:** (Level 26\) Programmed with "Temporal Predictive Logic" to lead moving targets into the center of the field.

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Core Chill:** The **Singularity Seed** is encased in the **Sub-Zero Chamber**. This "Thermal Null-Point" is required before the Seed is activated, or the heat from the engine would cause the stasis field to expand uncontrollably.
