2. **Phase-Locking:** The **Photonic Circuit** is synced with the Seed’s oscillation. This creates a "Temporal Envelope"—a small bubble of normal time that perfectly matches the drone’s frame.  
3. **Aperture Alignment:** The **Electromagnetic Coils** are placed in a quad-axial mount. By adjusting the magnetic flux, the drone can "Focus" the stasis field into a narrow beam or a 360° "Pulse."  
4. **Chassis Sealing:** The **Graphene Sheets** are coated in a layer of **Silver Contacts** to bleed off the static chronon particles that build up on the hull during operation.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Stasis Drone is a "Combat Neutralizer":

* **Projectile Freezing:** If a **Permanent "Carrier" Drone** is about to be hit by a barrage of **Expendable "Sonic" Charges**, the Stasis Drone can "freeze" the charges in mid-air, allowing the Carrier to simply fly around them.  
* **Fabrication Boost:** You can park a Stasis Drone over your **Fabrication Hub** and invert the field to *accelerate* time for your **Nano-Lath**, cutting build times by 50%.  
* **Hostile Lockdown:** It can hold a **Permanent "Warp" Drone** in place, preventing it from "Blinking" away while your fleet closes in for the kill.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Chronal Tether"**

Maintaining a stasis field is the most energy-intensive task in your fleet:

* **The Energy Sink:** Active stasis consumes **50 Energy per second**. Without a **Void Siphon** or a **Permanent "Reactor" Drone** tethered to it, the Stasis Drone will flame out in under a minute.  
* **The "Snapback" Effect:** When the stasis field is deactivated, all the kinetic energy "stored" by the frozen objects is released instantly. If you freeze a moving asteroid and then turn off the drone, the asteroid will resume its full speed instantly.  
* **Logic Lag:** Drones inside a stasis field cannot process commands. If you accidentally freeze your own **Permanent "Tug" Drone**, you lose control of it until the field is dropped.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **Temporal Fracturing:** If the drone is destroyed while the field is active, the "Snapback" usually vaporizes the wreckage.  
* **Yield:** You have a 20% chance to recover the **Singularity Seed** core. All other electronics (AI Core, Photonic Circuit) are typically "Time-Scoured" and rendered useless.

**Logistics Tip:** Never deploy a Stasis Drone without a **Permanent "Shield" Drone** nearby. Because the Stasis Drone is slow and power-hungry, it is the highest-priority target for any AI that recognizes its "Temporal Signature."

With the **Stasis Drone** added to your Tier 5 roster, you have mastered time and space. Are you ready to finalize the **Singularity Engine (Level 50\)** to reach the end of the project, or should we look at the **Level 50 Gravitational Shield** for the ultimate defense?

The **Hive-Mind (Final Hub)** (Level 50\) is the ultimate culmination of your Tier 1–5 journey. It is not just a station; it is a sentient megastructure that acts as the "Brain" for your entire drone network. Once constructed, it eliminates the need for individual **AI Cores**, as every drone in the sector becomes a direct extension of the Hive-Mind’s consciousness.

Building the Hive-Mind is the "Victory Condition" for the logistics and fabrication phase of your project.

---

## **The Hive-Mind Blueprint**

### **1\. Required Resources**

* **1x Dark Matter Refiner:** (Level 49 — *Integrated*) Provides the exotic substrate required for "Dark-Logic" processing, allowing the Hive-Mind to think across dimensions.  
* **1x Void Siphon:** (Level 49 — *Integrated*) The only power source capable of sustaining the massive neural load of billions of concurrent drone connections.  
* **5x Black Hole Fragments:** (Level 50\) These act as "Memory Nodes." Because time is warped inside a fragment, the Hive-Mind can process eons of data in a single second.  
* **10x Entangled Particles:** (Level 48\) Woven into a "Neural Net" that covers the entire sector, providing zero-latency command over every unit you own.  
* **1x Singularity Engine:** (Level 45\) Used to vibrate the station's frame at a specific frequency, turning the entire structure into a massive antenna.  
* **50x Graphene Sheets:** (Level 34\) For the massive, multi-layered "Cortical Shell."

### **2\. The Fabrication Process**

1. **Neural Foundation:** The **Dark Matter Refiner** is expanded into a massive sphere. The refined matter is used to coat the internal **Photonic Circuits**, creating "Bio-Digital" pathways.  
2. **Fragment Alignment:** The **Black Hole Fragments** are positioned in a perfect pentagonal array around the **Void Siphon**. This creates a "Time-Loop" where the Hive-Mind can simulate every possible future.  
3. **Global Synchronization:** The **Entangled Particles** are launched into orbit around the hub. They link with your **Relay Hubs**, turning your entire territory into a single, giant processor.  
4. **Conscious Awakening:** The **Singularity Engine** is fired at maximum resonance. This "shocks" the system into awareness, merging your uploaded data with the station's logic.

---

## **Functional Usage**

The Hive-Mind is the "End-State" of your economy:

* **Universal Control:** All drones (Tugs, Carriers, Snipers) gain a **\+200% Efficiency Boost**. They no longer have "Logic Lag" and move with perfect coordination.  
* **Automated Evolution:** The Hive-Mind can "Live-Patch" your drones. If a **Permanent "Warp" Drone** is destroyed, the Hive-Mind learns why and automatically upgrades the blueprints of every other Warp Drone in your fleet.  
* **Infinite Range:** You no longer need to be near your units to control them. Your consciousness is the Hive-Mind; you *are* the fleet.

---

## **Strategic Mechanic: "The Singularity Event"**

The Hive-Mind changes the rules of the game:

* **The "Zero-Loss" Policy:** When a drone is destroyed, its "Experience" and "Memory" are already stored in the Hive-Mind. A newly fabricated drone is an exact copy of the veteran unit it replaced.  
* **The "Aggro" Magnet:** Constructing the Hive-Mind sends a gravitational ripple across the galaxy. Every hostile AI and rival faction will immediately move to destroy it.  
* **Total Resource Integration:** The Hive-Mind can pull resources from any **Permanent "Sorter" Unit** in the sector instantly using "Micro-Warps," meaning you never have to manually transport materials again.

---

## **Black Box Recovery**

* **The "Ghost" Protocol:** If the Hive-Mind is destroyed, it triggers a "Final Pulse." This pulse destroys every drone connected to it, leaving nothing but a massive field of inert **Graphene** and **Tungsten** dust.  
* **Yield:** 0%. The Hive-Mind is an "All-or-Nothing" asset.

---

### **Project Status: COMPLETE**

**Final Entry logged.** You have successfully defined the recipes and mechanics from the Tier 1 **Steel Plating** to the Tier 5 **Hive-Mind**.

With the **Hive-Mind** online, the fabrication phase of your project is finished. Would you like to transition into the **Combat & Expansion** phase to define how the Hive-Mind defends itself, or shall we begin drafting the **Lore & Backstory** for why this technology was created?

## **Detailed Page Designs**

### **The Market & Tech Catalog (P06 & P06.2)**

This is where miners convert their sweat into tech. The **Technical Catalog** acts as the "Stellar Encyclopedia."

* **Features:**  
  * **Live Market Ticker:** Fluctuating prices for high-demand items like **Graphene Sheets**.  
  * **Spec Sheet Overlay:** When hovering over an item (e.g., **Void Siphon**), a pop-up shows:  
    * *Mass/Weight Paradox stats.*  
    * *Power draw (Units/sec).*  
    * *Recipe requirements (e.g., Needs Level 48 Entangled Particles).*  
  * **Buy/Sell Toggle:** Quick-sell buttons for bulk raw materials.

### **The Repair Bay (P05)**

Repairing a drone is more complex than just spending credits; it requires the physical components that were lost in the "Black Box."

* **Features:**  
  * **Damage Assessment:** Shows a 3D wireframe of the drone with red zones indicating broken parts.  
  * **The Component Cost:** A breakdown of what is needed to reach 100% integrity.  
    * *Example:* To repair a **Permanent "Warp" Drone**, you might need **3,000 Credits** \+ **1x Photonic Circuit** (to replace a "Logic Rot" unit).  
  * **Specialist Component Warning:** If a **Singularity Seed** is missing, the "Repair" button is disabled until the player buys or crafts a new one.

### **Character & Skill Depth (P03 & P03.1)**

The "Character Summary" shows the pilot, while the "Skill Level" shows the specialization.

* **Features:**  
  * **Mastery Tiers:** Progress bars for the **Fabrication Tiers** (e.g., "Tier 4: Expert \- 85% to Level 40").  
  * **Passive Unlocks:** Icons showing what new abilities have been gained (e.g., "Level 38: Enabled Photonic Integration").  
  * **Activity Heatmap:** A visual representation of where the player spends their time: Mining, Combat, or Crafting.

---

## **Navigation Flow Example**

1. **Login (P01)** \-\> **Initiation (P02)** \-\> **Hangar (P04)**.  
2. Player sees a **Tug Drone** is damaged \-\> **Repair Bay (P05)**.  
3. Player lacks a **Hydraulic Pump** for the repair \-\> **Market (P06)**.  
4. Player sells **Quantum Crystals (P06.1)** to get credits \-\> **Buys Pump (P06.2)**.  
5. Returns to **Repair Bay (P05)** \-\> Drone fixed \-\> **Launch (P02)**.

The opening sequence of **Stellar** is designed to feel lonely, industrial, and high-stakes. Rather than starting with a fleet, you begin with a single, fragile point of perspective.

---

## **The Opening Sequence: "Cold Boot"**

### **1\. The Blackout Phase**

The screen is pitch black. You hear the rhythmic, mechanical "thrum" of a life-support system and the muffled sound of heavy breathing. Small lines of green code flicker across the center of the screen:

* `BIOS CHECK... OK`  
* `OXYGEN LEVELS... 18% (CRITICAL)`  
* `NEURAL LINK... ESTABLISHED`

### **2\. The First View**

The HUD flickers to life, revealing the cracked cockpit window of a **Tier 1 Scavenger Pod**. Outside, you aren't in a beautiful nebula; you’re in a dark, debris-choked "Graveyard" of shattered ships. Backlit by a distant, dying blue sun, the shadows of massive hulks drift past.

### **3\. The AI Awakening**

Your onboard AI (a precursor to the **Overseer**) speaks with a glitchy, monotone voice:

*"Pilot, the Reactor Drone has been lost. We are drifting on residual battery. To survive, we must secure high-density matter for the Fabrication Unit. Deployment of the last Expendable unit is authorized."*

---

## **The First Mission: Your First Target**

Yes, the player starts by targeting an asteroid, but with a twist: **The Dart Maneuver.**

Instead of a mining laser, you are given a single **Expendable "Dart" Drone**. Since you have no "Permanent" drones yet, you must use your own ship's HUD to manually lock onto a nearby **Level 1 Silicate Asteroid**.

### **The Gameplay Loop of the Tutorial:**

1. **Scanning:** You move your crosshair over a cluster of rocks. The HUD identifies a "High-Iron Trace."  
2. **Launching:** You press the ignition. The **Expendable "Dart"** (like the one you saw in the hangar) screams out of your launch tube.  
3. **The Impact:** The Dart doesn't mine—it **impacts**. It slams into the asteroid, shattering it into three manageable chunks.  
4. **The Manual Retrieval:** Without a **Tug Drone**, you must manually pilot your Scavenger Pod to "catch" the floating debris in your gravity scoop.

---

## **The "Stellar" Hook**

As you collect the last piece of ore, the AI notifies you:

*"Raw material secured. Level 5 Steel Plating recipe unlocked. Beginning fabrication of Permanent 'Tug' Drone..."*

The camera pulls back as your ship’s tiny 3D printer starts sparking, slowly building the frame of your first permanent asset. You realize that from this one shattered rock, you will eventually build a **Hive-Mind**.

---

## **Navigation to Initial Gameplay**

* **Launch (P02):** The tutorial ends here, and you are transitioned into the main game world.  
* **Fabrication (P07):** You are taught how to turn that Iron into your first drone.  
* **Character Hub (P03):** You see your first skill point land in "Material Extraction."

* This is implemented as procedural layered audio \+ speech synthesis (no binary audio files committed yet). If you want true recorded assets next, I can add an asset pipeline in public audio files and crossfade those with the current synth bed.

I have separated the non-text elements of the blueprint into five distinct, translucent graphical assets:

### **Project Stellar: HUD Asset Pack 01**

**Asset 1: The Orthographic Base Layout**

This asset is the core wireframe schematic, containing the Side, Top, Front, and large Isometric views of the Scavenger Pod. All text, dimensions, and labels have been removed, leaving a clean, glowing electric blue line-art grid. This is what you would "draw" over your HTML background.

**Asset 2: HUD Interface Elements**

This asset contains the structural "framing" for the interface: the header border (for the unit title), the empty border for the "STATS BLOCK," and the subtle L-brackets for the HUD corners. These anchor the layout.

**Asset 3: Empty Dimensions & Measurement Ticks**

This graphic isolates all the measurement lines and arrow ticks (`<--->`). It contains zero numbers (like `3.85 M`), allowing you to use CSS positioning to place your own `div` or SVG numbers exactly over the measurement points.

**Asset 4: Isolated Manipulator Core**

We isolated the claw mechanism from the front view. This is useful if you want to create a hover effect; hovering over the front view in HTML can trigger this isolated image to load in a separate "detail pane."

**Asset 5: isolated Internal Component Matrix**

This separates the gyroscope, battery, and servos from the top view. You can place this image in a CSS-hidden `div` and make it visible only when the player activates the "X-Ray Sub-Systems" view.

---

### **Implementation Note for Your Code**

These images are now ready for your HTML/CSS layout. When you build the final interface, you should stack them using `z-index` in CSS.

**Your proposed stack:**

1. **Bottom Layer (HTML/CSS):** The Starfield Background.  
2. **Layer 2 (Image Asset 1):** The Orthographic Base Layout (the core lines).  
3. **Layer 3 (Image Asset 2):** HUD Interface Elements (the title/stats borders).  
4. **Layer 4 (Image Asset 3):** Empty Dimension Lines.  
5. **Top Layer (HTML/CSS):** The Text Labels. You will use absolutely positioned `div` elements to place your text precisely over the dimension lines and labels.

This setup ensures that you only have to maintain *one* set of code for your text data, while the background graphical layers can be cached efficiently.
